#Dubois 1: Zoo inauguration

dubois.1 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.1.t

	desc = dubois.1.d

	flavor = dubois.1.f

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_diplomatic_action.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		owner = {
			set_variable = dubois_zoo_inauguration_happened
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = dubois_naturalist_var }
			var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
				set_variable = dubois_naturalist_inaugurated_zoo_var
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1.g
		default_option = yes
		dubois_add_x_academy_progress = {
			AMOUNT = "5"
		}
		set_variable = dubois_visiting_zoo_var
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = { 
				id = dubois.1001
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lepsius.10.h #Have a nice day
		dubois_add_x_academy_progress = {
			AMOUNT = "5"
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Dubois 2: Origin of Species

dubois.2 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.2.t

	desc = dubois.2.d

	flavor = dubois.2.f

	placement = ROOT

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:dubois_naturalist_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	trigger = {
		has_technology_researched = dubois_theory_of_evolution_tech
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = dubois_theory_of_evolution
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = dubois_theory_of_evolution
		if = {
			limit ={
				NOT = {
					has_variable = dubois_naturalist_var
				}
			}
			create_new_naturalist_effect = yes
			dubois_set_new_naturalist_as_naturalist_effect = yes
		}
		var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
			save_scope_as = dubois_naturalist_scope
			set_variable = dubois_invented_evolution_theory_var
		}
		set_variable = dubois_first_inventor_evolution_theory_var
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.2.g
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = dubois_theory_of_evolution_invented_modifier
			years = 5
		}
		dubois_large_add_technology = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.2.h
		add_modifier = {
			name = dubois_theory_of_evolution_invented_modifier
			years = 5
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = state_atheism_conversion_tt
			every_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					is_incorporated = yes
				}
				convert_population = {
					target = rel:atheist
					value = 0.05
				}
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Dubois 3: Return of the Beagle

dubois.3 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.3.t

	desc = dubois.3.d

	flavor = dubois.3.f

	placement = ROOT

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:dubois_naturalist_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			game_date >= 1837.1.1
		}
		ROOT = c:GBR
		NOT = {
			has_variable = dubois_beagle_returned
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = dubois_beagle_returned
		create_darwin_effect = yes
		var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
			save_scope_as = dubois_naturalist_scope
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.3.g
		default_option = yes
		dubois_add_x_specimen_effect = { AMOUNT = 5000 }
		dubois_add_x_fossils_effect = { AMOUNT = 3 }
		dubois_medium_add_technology = yes
		remove_modifier = rapanui_pacific_expedition_modifier
		add_modifier = {
			name = rapanui_had_pacific_expedition_modifier
			years = 5
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Dubois 4: Kosmos

dubois.4 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.4.t

	desc = dubois.4.d

	flavor = dubois.4.f

	placement = ROOT

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_humboldt.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	trigger = {
		game_date >= 1845.1.1
		NOT = {
			game_date >= 1846.1.1
		}
		exists = c:PRU
		ROOT = c:PRU
		NOT = {
			has_variable = dubois_kosmos_published
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = dubois_kosmos_published
		create_new_naturalist_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.4.g
		default_option = yes
		dubois_large_add_technology = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			dubois_remove_new_naturalist_effect = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.4.h
		if = {
			limit ={
				NOT = {
					has_variable = dubois_naturalist_var
				}
			}
			dubois_set_new_naturalist_as_naturalist_effect = yes
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Dubois 5: Mendel

dubois.5 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.5.t

	desc = dubois.5.d

	flavor = dubois.5.f

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_mendel.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	trigger = {
		game_date >= 1900.1.1
		NOT = {
			game_date >= 1901.1.1
		}
		exists = c:AUS
		ROOT = c:AUS
		has_technology_researched = dubois_genetics_tech
		NOT = {
			has_variable = dubois_mendel_rediscovered
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = dubois_mendel_rediscovered
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.5.g
		default_option = yes
		dubois_large_add_technology = yes
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Dubois 6: Dubois finds the Java Man (alternative to Rapanui.250)

dubois.6 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.6.t
	desc = dubois.6.d
	flavor = dubois.6.f

	placement = scope:dubois_java_man_location

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_fossil_java.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fossil.dds"

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = dubois_java_man_found
		}
		game_date >= 1891.1.1
		has_technology_researched = dubois_paleontology_tech
		exists = c:NET
		ROOT = c:NET
	}

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = dubois_java_man_found
		random_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_EAST_JAVA
			}
			save_scope_as = dubois_java_man_location
		}

		create_dubois_eugene_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = rapanui.250.g #A historical day
		default_option = yes
		dubois_add_fossil_java = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_variable = lepsius_erectus_systemized
				}
			}
			set_global_variable = lepsius_erectus_systemized
			set_variable = lepsius_erectus_systemizer
			lepsius_change_anthropological_rating = {
				AMOUNT = 100
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				lepsius_add_erectus_fossil_effect = yes
				lepsius_add_erectus_fossil_effect = yes
				lepsius_add_erectus_fossil_effect = yes
			}
		}
		else = {
			lepsius_change_anthropological_rating = {
				AMOUNT = 50
			}
		}

		dubois_medium_add_technology = yes
		paleontologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "75"
		}
		post_notification = dubois_java_man_notification

		hidden_effect = {
			dubois_remove_new_paleontologist_effect = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.6.g #We need this man as our lead palaeontologist!
		dubois_add_fossil_java = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_variable = lepsius_erectus_systemized
				}
			}
			set_global_variable = lepsius_erectus_systemized
			set_variable = lepsius_erectus_systemizer
			lepsius_change_anthropological_rating = {
				AMOUNT = 100
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				lepsius_add_erectus_fossil_effect = yes
				lepsius_add_erectus_fossil_effect = yes
				lepsius_add_erectus_fossil_effect = yes
			}
		}
		
		post_notification = dubois_java_man_notification

		dubois_set_new_paleontologist_as_paleontologist_effect = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Dubois 7: The Peppered Moth evolves!

dubois.7 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.7.t
	desc = dubois.7.d
	flavor = dubois.7.f

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_evolution_peppered_moth.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = dubois_peppered_moth_evolved_var
		}
		dubois_has_naturalist = yes
		has_technology_researched = dubois_theory_of_evolution_tech
		any_scope_state = {
			pollution_generation > 2000
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = dubois_peppered_moth_evolved_var
	}

	option = {	#Clear evidence for evolution!
		name = dubois.7.g

		naturalist_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = 10 }
		var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
			set_variable = dubois_naturalist_showed_evolution_in_peppered_moths_var
		}
		dubois_medium_add_technology = yes
	}
}


######Diplomatic action######

#Dubois 11: Diplomatic Action, Animal selection

dubois.11 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.11.t

	desc = dubois.11.d

	flavor = dubois.11.f

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_diplomatic_action.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	trigger = {

	}

	immediate = {
		scope:target_country = {
			save_scope_as = dubois_animal_country
		}
	}
	######NORTH AMERICA######

	#Grizzly Bear
	option = {
		name = dubois.11.grizzly
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = dubois_zoo_animal_grizzly
					has_variable = dubois_transport_grizzly
				}
				scope:target_country = {
					any_scope_state = {
						has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_grizzly_habitat
					}
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = dubois_zoo_animal_transport_tt
		set_variable = dubois_transport_grizzly
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.102
				days = { 30 60 }
			}
		}
	}
	#Bald Eagle
	option = {
		name = dubois.11.eagle
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = dubois_zoo_animal_eagle
					has_variable = dubois_transport_eagle
				}
				scope:target_country = {
					any_scope_state = {
						has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_eagle_habitat
					}
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = dubois_zoo_animal_transport_tt
		set_variable = dubois_transport_eagle
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.103
				days = { 30 60 }
			}
		}
	}
	#Bison
	option = {
		name = dubois.11.bison
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = dubois_zoo_animal_bison
					has_variable = dubois_transport_bison
				}
				scope:target_country = {

#Dubois 12: Smuggle succeeds

	type = country_event

	title = dubois.12.t

	desc = dubois.12.d

	flavor = dubois.12.f

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_diplomatic_action.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	trigger = {

	}

	immediate = {
		scope:target_country = {
			save_scope_as = dubois_animal_country
		}

#Dubois 13: Smuggle fails

dubois.13 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.13.t

	desc = dubois.13.d

	flavor = dubois.13.f

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_diplomatic_action.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	trigger = {

	}

	immediate = {
		scope:target_country = {
			save_scope_as = dubois_animal_country
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dubois.13.g #That didn't work as intended
		default_option = yes
		change_infamy = 10
		add_modifier = {
			name = dubois_poacher_modifier
			years = 10
		}
		scope:dubois_animal_country = {
			change_relations = {
				country = ROOT 
				value = -25
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		remove_variable = dubois_smuggle_zoo_animal_var
	}
}

######Catch local animals######

#Dubois 21: Collect animals

dubois.21 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.21.t

	desc = dubois.21.d

	flavor = dubois.21.f

	placement = ROOT

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:dubois_naturalist_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		dubois_calculate_catch_animals = yes
		var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
			save_scope_as = dubois_naturalist_scope
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.21.g
		default_option = yes
		remove_modifier = dubois_search_local_animal_modifier
		dubois_add_total_catch_animals = yes
		naturalist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "25"
		}
	}

	after = {
		dubois_remove_catch_animals = yes
		scope:dubois_naturalist_scope = {
			remove_modifier = dubois_animal_hunter_modifier
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = no
		}
	}
}

#Dubois 31: Safari starts

dubois.31 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.31.t

	desc = dubois.31.d

	flavor = dubois.31.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_safari.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/middleeast/jungle_expedition"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
			save_scope_as = dubois_naturalist_scope
		}
		dubois_set_safari_progress = yes
		dubois_set_safari_trap = yes
		dubois_set_safari_track = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.31.g #Hippopotamus
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_variable = dubois_zoo_animal_hippopotamus
			}
			any_state = {
				has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_hippopotamus_habitat
				OR = {
					owner = {
						is_country_type = decentralized
					}
					owner = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dubois_safari_hippopotamus
			value = 1
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.31.h #Lion
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_variable = dubois_zoo_animal_lion
			}
			any_state = {
				has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_lion_habitat
				OR = {
					owner = {
						is_country_type = decentralized
					}
					owner = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dubois_safari_lion
			value = 1
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.31.i #Elephant
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_variable = dubois_zoo_animal_elephant
			}
			any_state = {
				has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_elefant_habitat
				OR = {
					owner = {
						is_country_type = decentralized
					}
					owner = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dubois_safari_elephant
			value = 1
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.31.j #Giraffe
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_variable = dubois_zoo_animal_giraffe
			}
			any_state = {
				has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_giraffe_habitat
				OR = {
					owner = {
						is_country_type = decentralized
					}
					owner = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dubois_safari_giraffe
			value = 1
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.31.k #Zebra
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_variable = dubois_zoo_animal_zebra
			}
			any_state = {
				has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_zebra_habitat
				OR = {
					owner = {
						is_country_type = decentralized
					}
					owner = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dubois_safari_zebra
			value = 1
		}
	}

	after = {
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = je_dubois_safari
		}
	}
}

#Dubois 32: Standard event: Trap or Follow

dubois.32 = {
	type = country_event

	title = {
		triggered_desc = {

		}

			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_safari_giraffe
				var:dubois_safari_flavor_randomizer = 1
			}
			desc = dubois.32.f.giraffe.1
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_safari_giraffe
				var:dubois_safari_flavor_randomizer = 2
			}
			desc = dubois.32.f.giraffe.2
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_safari_giraffe
				var:dubois_safari_flavor_randomizer = 3
			}
			desc = dubois.32.f.giraffe.3
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_safari_zebra
				var:dubois_safari_flavor_randomizer = 1
			}
			desc = dubois.32.f.zebra.1
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_safari_zebra
				var:dubois_safari_flavor_randomizer = 2
			}
			desc = dubois.32.f.zebra.2
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_safari_zebra
				var:dubois_safari_flavor_randomizer = 3
			}
			desc = dubois.32.f.zebra.3
		}
	}

	duration = 1

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_safari.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/middleeast/jungle_expedition"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	trigger = {
		var:dubois_safari_progress <= 4
	}

	immediate = {
		var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
			save_scope_as = dubois_naturalist_scope
		}

		random_list = { #randomizes flavor text
			1 = { 
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_safari_flavor_randomizer
					value = 1
				}
			}
			1 = { 
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_safari_flavor_randomizer
					value = 2
				}
			}
			1 = { 
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_safari_flavor_randomizer
					value = 3
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.32.g #Trap
		default_option = yes
		dubois_add_safari_trap = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.32.h #Track
		dubois_add_safari_track = yes
	}

	after = {
		dubois_add_safari_progress = yes

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dubois_safari_hippopotamus
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = dubois_safari_hippopotamus
				add = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dubois_safari_lion
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = dubois_safari_lion
				add = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dubois_safari_elephant
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = dubois_safari_elephant
				add = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dubois_safari_giraffe
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = dubois_safari_giraffe
				add = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dubois_safari_zebra
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = dubois_safari_zebra
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

#Dubois 38: Safari Hidden

dubois.38 = {
	type = country_event

	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		var:dubois_safari_progress = 5
		NOR = {
			AND = {
				has_variable = dubois_safari_hippopotamus
				var:dubois_safari_trap >= 3
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = dubois_safari_lion
				var:dubois_safari_trap >= 2
				var:dubois_safari_track >= 2
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = dubois_safari_elephant
				var:dubois_safari_trap >= 4
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = dubois_safari_giraffe
				var:dubois_safari_trap >= 2
				var:dubois_safari_track >= 1
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = dubois_safari_zebra
				var:dubois_safari_trap >= 1
				var:dubois_safari_track >= 2
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		dubois_add_safari_progress = yes
		set_variable = dubois_safari_fail
	}
}

dubois.39 = {

	title = dubois.39.t

	desc = dubois.39.d

			}
			desc = dubois.40.d.success
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_safari_fail
			}
			desc = dubois.40.d.fail
		}
	}

	flavor = dubois.40.f

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_safari.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
			save_scope_as = dubois_naturalist_scope
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.40.g #
		default_option = yes
		remove_modifier = dubois_on_safari_modifier
		add_modifier = {
			name = dubois_had_safari_modifier
			years = 3
		}
	}

	after = {
		dubois_remove_safari_effect = yes
		scope:dubois_naturalist_scope = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = no
			remove_modifier = dubois_animal_hunter_modifier
		}
	}
}

######ADDITIONAL AFRICA EXPEDITION EVENTS######

#Dubois 41: Exotic plants

dubois.41 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.41.t
	desc = dubois.41.d
	flavor = dubois.41.f

	placement = scope:current_expedition_location

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		video = "middleeast_jungle_expedition"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"

	cooldown = { 
		months = 6
	}

	trigger = {
		var:expedition_progress >= 1
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = congo_river_expedition_var }
			congo_river_expedition_location = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_variable = niger_river_expedition_var }
			niger_river_expedition_location = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_variable = central_africa_expedition_var }
			central_africa_location_effect = yes
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = { has_variable = expedition_leader_var }
			save_scope_as = expedition_leader
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.41.g #Collect some plants
		default_option = yes
		dubois_add_x_specimen_effect = { AMOUNT = 1000 }
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.41.h #Collect as many plants as possible
		dubois_add_x_specimen_effect = { AMOUNT = 3000 }
		dubois_small_add_technology = yes
		random_list = {
			65 = {}
			35 = { add_small_peril_effect = yes }
		}
	}
}

	type = country_event

	desc = dubois.44.d
	flavor = dubois.44.f

	event_image = {
		video = "middleeast_jungle_expedition"
	}

		months = 6
	}

		var:expedition_progress >= 1
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = congo_river_expedition_var }
			congo_river_expedition_location = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_variable = niger_river_expedition_var }
			niger_river_expedition_location = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_variable = central_africa_expedition_var }
			central_africa_location_effect = yes
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = { has_variable = expedition_leader_var }
			save_scope_as = expedition_leader
		}
		ig:ig_intelligentsia = {
			save_scope_as = intelligentsia_ig
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.44.g #Return and regain the samples
		dubois_add_x_specimen_effect = { AMOUNT = 5000 }
		expedition_lose_progress_effect = yes
		add_small_peril_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.44.h #Leave this worthless trash behind
		default_option = yes
		scope:intelligentsia_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = ig_not_placated
				years = 3
			}
		}
	}
}

			limit = { has_variable = congo_river_expedition_var }
			congo_river_expedition_location = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_variable = niger_river_expedition_var }
			niger_river_expedition_location = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_variable = central_africa_expedition_var }
			central_africa_location_effect = yes
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = { has_variable = expedition_leader_var }
			save_scope_as = expedition_leader
		}
		ig:ig_intelligentsia = {
			save_scope_as = intelligentsia_ig
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.45.g #We buy the collection
		default_option = yes
		dubois_add_x_specimen_effect = { AMOUNT = 3000 }
		add_treasury = -25000
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.45.h #We are more interested in his knowledge
		dubois_small_add_technology = yes
		add_treasury = -25000
	}
}

######FORMATIONS######

#Dubois 71: Add Formations

dubois.71 = {
	type = country_event

	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = dubois_formations_set_var
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = dubois_formations_set_var

		dubois_add_normal_formations = yes

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = dubois_historical_formations_rule
			}
			dubois_add_historical_great_formations = yes
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = dubois_random_formations_rule
			}
			dubois_add_random_great_formations = yes
		}
	}
}

#Dubois 72: Normal Formation discovered

dubois.72 = {
	type = country_event

    title = dubois.72.t
		
    desc = dubois.72.d

	flavor = dubois.72.f

	placement = scope:dubois_formation_state

	duration = 1
		
	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_fossil_scaphognathus.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airship"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fossil.dds"

	trigger = {
		any_scope_state = {
			has_variable = dubois_has_normal_formation_var
			NOT = {
				has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_normal_formation
			}
		}
		dubois_can_discover_formation = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dubois_has_normal_formation_var
				NOT = {
					has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_normal_formation
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = dubois_formation_state
		}
	}

	option = { #We should inspect that formation
		name = dubois.72.g
		default_option = yes
		scope:dubois_formation_state = {
			state_region = {
				add_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_normal_formation
			}
		}
	}
}

#Dubois 73: Great Formation discovered

dubois.73 = {
	type = country_event

    title = dubois.73.t
		
    desc = dubois.73.d

	flavor = dubois.72.f

	placement = scope:dubois_formation_state

	duration = 1
		
	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_fossil_scaphognathus.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airship"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fossil.dds"

	trigger = {
		any_scope_state = {
			has_variable = dubois_has_great_formation_var
			NOR = {
				has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_north_american_formation
				has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_south_american_formation
				has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_european_formation
				has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_african_formation
				has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_asian_formation
				has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_australian_formation
			}
		}
		dubois_can_discover_formation = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dubois_has_great_formation_var
				NOR = {
					has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_north_american_formation
					has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_south_american_formation
					has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_european_formation
					has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_african_formation
					has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_asian_formation
					has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_australian_formation
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = dubois_formation_state
		}
	}

	option = { #We should inspect that formation
		name = dubois.72.g
		default_option = yes
		scope:dubois_formation_state = {
			#NORTH AMERICA
			if = {
				limit = {
					state_is_in_north_america = yes
				}
				state_region = {
					add_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_north_american_formation
				}
			}
			#SOUTH AMERICA
			if = {
				limit = {
					state_is_in_south_america = yes
				}
				state_region = {
					add_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_south_american_formation
				}
			}
			#EUROPE
			if = {
				limit = {
					state_is_in_europe = yes
				}
				state_region = {
					add_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_european_formation
				}
			}
			#AFRICA
			if = {
				limit = {
					state_is_in_africa = yes
				}
				state_region = {
					add_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_african_formation
				}
			}
			#ASIA
			if = {
				limit = {
					state_is_in_east_asia = yes
				}
				state_region = {
					add_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_asian_formation
				}
			}
			#AUSTRALIA
			if = {
				limit = {
					region = sr:region_oceania
				}
				state_region = {
					add_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_australian_formation
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#######BOTANY

#Dubois 82: Yearly botanical report

dubois.82 = {
	type = country_event
		
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = dubois_botanical_report_cooldown_var
		}
		dubois_botanical_research = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = dubois_botanical_report_cooldown_var
			days = 365
		}
		dubois_add_x_specimen_effect = { AMOUNT = 1000 } #base specimen

		#Additional yearly specimen
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_type = building_university
					has_active_production_method = pm_dubois_university_natural_history
				}
			}
			dubois_add_x_specimen_effect = { AMOUNT = 1000 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
					var:dubois_naturalist_experience >= 100
				}
			}
			dubois_add_x_specimen_effect = { AMOUNT = 1000 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
					var:dubois_naturalist_experience >= 200
				}
			}
			dubois_add_x_specimen_effect = { AMOUNT = 1000 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
					var:dubois_naturalist_experience >= 300
				}
			}
			dubois_add_x_specimen_effect = { AMOUNT = 1000 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dubois_yearly_specimen_var
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = dubois_specimen_notification_var
				value = var:dubois_yearly_specimen_var
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = dubois_yearly_specimen_var
				value = 0
			}
		}

		#Notification
		if = {
			limit = {
				dubois_botanical_research = yes
			}
			post_notification = dubois_botanical_report_notification
		}
	}
}

#####################################################################

######PALEONTOLOGY######

#Dubois 200: Opening of the Natural History Museum

dubois.200 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.200.t

	desc = dubois.200.d

	flavor = dubois.200.f

	placement = ROOT

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fossil.dds"

	trigger = {
		has_technology_researched = dubois_paleontology_tech
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = dubois_paleontology_invented
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = dubois_paleontology_invented
		if = {
			limit ={
				NOT = {
					has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_var
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					c:GBR ?= this
					NOT = {
						has_global_variable = dubois_owen_created_var
					}
				}
				create_owen_richard_effect = yes
			}
			else = {
				create_new_paleontologist_effect = yes
				dubois_set_new_paleontologist_as_paleontologist_effect = yes
			}
		}
		var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = dubois_paleontologist_scope
			set_variable = dubois_paleontologist_opened_first_paleontological_museum_var
		}
	}

	option = { #That sounds like a great place to visit!
		name = dubois.200.g
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = dubois_natural_history_museum_modifier
			years = 5
		}
		
		dubois_add_x_fossils_effect = { AMOUNT = 3 }
	}

	after = {
	}
}

	}

		ig:ig_petty_bourgeoisie = {
			save_scope_as = petty_bourgeoisie_ig

				save_scope_as = pb_leader

#Dubois 205: Bones in the mineshaft

dubois.205 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.205.t
	desc = dubois.205.d
	flavor = dubois.205.f

	placement = scope:dubois_excavation_state

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_fossil_mixed.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fossil.dds"

	cooldown = { 
		years = 15
	}

	trigger = {
		dubois_paleontological_research = yes
		any_scope_state = {
			OR = {
				has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_normal_formation
				has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_north_american_formation
				has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_south_american_formation
				has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_european_formation
				has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_african_formation
				has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_asian_formation
				has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_australian_formation
			}
			OR = {
				has_building = building_coal_mine
				has_building = building_iron_mine
				has_building = building_lead_mine
				has_building = building_sulfur_mine
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_normal_formation
					has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_north_american_formation
					has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_south_american_formation
					has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_european_formation
					has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_african_formation
					has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_asian_formation
					has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_australian_formation
				}
				OR = {
					has_building = building_coal_mine
					has_building = building_iron_mine
					has_building = building_lead_mine
					has_building = building_sulfur_mine
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = dubois_excavation_state
		}
		ig:ig_industrialists = {
			save_scope_as = industralists_ig
		}
		ig:ig_intelligentsia = {
			save_scope_as = intelligentsia_ig
		}
		var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = dubois_paleontologist_scope
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.205.g #We must have these fossils at all costs.
		dubois_add_x_fossils_effect = { AMOUNT = 5 }
		paleontologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "25"
		}
		scope:dubois_excavation_state = {
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				strata = rich
				value = medium_radicals
			}
		}
		scope:industralists_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = ig_not_placated
				years = 5
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.205.h #Our scientists may examine the place but should not excavate the mine.
		default_option = yes
		dubois_small_add_technology = yes
		paleontologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "15"
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.205.i #Don't disturb these gentlemen.
		scope:intelligentsia_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = ig_not_placated
				years = 2
			}
		}
		scope:industralists_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = ig_placated
				years = 5
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

	}

	trigger = {
		dubois_paleontological_research = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = dubois_paleontologist_scope
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.207.g #So exciting.
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = dubois_fossil_trilobite
				}
			}
			dubois_add_fossil_trilobite = yes
		}
		dubois_add_x_fossils_effect = { AMOUNT = 1 }
		dubois_small_add_technology = yes
		paleontologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "25"
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Dubois 208: Ammonites

dubois.208 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.208.t
	desc = dubois.208.d
	flavor = dubois.208.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_fossil_mixed.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fossil.dds"

	cooldown = { 
		years = 20
	}

	trigger = {
		dubois_paleontological_research = yes
		any_scope_state = {
			OR = {
				has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_normal_formation
				has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_north_american_formation
				has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_south_american_formation
				has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_european_formation
				has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_african_formation
				has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_asian_formation
				has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_australian_formation
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_normal_formation
					has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_north_american_formation
					has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_south_american_formation
					has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_european_formation
					has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_african_formation
					has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_asian_formation
					has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_great_australian_formation
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = dubois_excavation_state
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.208.g #So exciting.
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = dubois_fossil_ammonite
				}
			}
			dubois_add_fossil_ammonite = yes
		}
		dubois_add_x_fossils_effect = { AMOUNT = 3 }
		paleontologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "25"
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

######Dinosaur Bones######

#Dubois 211: Dinosaur Excavation

dubois.211 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.211.t
	desc = dubois.211.d
	flavor = dubois.211.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_dinosaur_quarry.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fossil.dds"

	cooldown = { 
		years = 3
	}

	trigger = {
		dubois_paleontological_research = yes
		dubois_has_potential_dinosaur_bone = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		dubois_set_dinosaur_excavation_progress = yes
		var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = dubois_paleontologist_scope
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.211.g #Get your shovels!
		dubois_add_dinousaur_bone = yes
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = je_dubois_dinosaur_excavation
		}
	}

	after = {
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			has_technology_researched = dubois_paleontology_tech
		  	factor = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
				var:dubois_paleontologist_experience >= 25
			}
		  	factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
				var:dubois_paleontologist_experience >= 50
			}
		  	factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
				var:dubois_paleontologist_experience >= 100
			}
		  	factor = 3
		}
		modifier = {
			var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
				var:dubois_paleontologist_experience >= 150
			}
		  	factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
				var:dubois_paleontologist_experience >= 200
			}
		  	factor = 3
		}
		modifier = {
			var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
				var:dubois_paleontologist_experience >= 250
			}
		  	factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
				var:dubois_paleontologist_experience >= 300
			}
		  	factor = 3
		}
	}
}

		years = 100
	}

	trigger = {
		dubois_paleontological_research = yes
		dubois_dinosaur_research_in_north_america = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = dubois_paleontologist_scope
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.221.g #So exciting.
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = dubois_fossil_smilodon
				}
			}
			dubois_add_fossil_smilodon = yes
		}
		dubois_add_x_fossils_effect = { AMOUNT = 1 }
		dubois_medium_add_technology = yes
		paleontologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "35"
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Dubois 233: Local Paleontologist shares Research
dubois.233 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.233.t
	desc = dubois.233.d
	flavor = dubois.233.f

	duration = 3

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fossil.dds"

	cooldown = { 
		years = 50
	}

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		create_character = {
			trait_generation = {}
			age = { 55 90 }
			save_scope_as = dubois_paleontologist_scope
		}
		scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope = {
			add_trait = dubois_paleontologist
			set_variable = mr_is_paleontologist_var
			mr_trait_generation_paleontologist_effect = yes
			place_character_in_void = 4
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.233.g #This is an amazing collection!
		
		dubois_add_x_paleontological_progress_effect = { AMOUNT = 50 }
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Dubois 301: Botanical Expedition Destinantion

dubois.301 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.301.t
	desc = dubois.301.d
	flavor = dubois.301.f

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:dubois_naturalist_scope

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_botany.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
			save_scope_as = dubois_naturalist_scope
		}
	}

	option = {	#To Amazonas
		name = dubois.301.g
		trigger = {
			dubois_botanical_expedition_possible_amazonas = yes
			NOR = {
				has_modifier = dubois_botanical_expedition_modifier
				has_modifier = dubois_naturalist_travell_to_location_modifier
				has_modifier = dubois_naturalist_travell_from_location_modifier
			}
			scope:dubois_naturalist_scope = {
				is_busy = no
			}
		}
		scope:dubois_naturalist_scope = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
		dubois_set_naturalist_to_amazonas = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = dubois_botanical_expedition_modifier
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = dubois_botanical_expedition_cost_modifier
			multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_very_small
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = dubois_naturalist_travell_to_location_modifier
			days = 90
		}
	}

	option = {	#To Congo
		name = dubois.301.h
		trigger = {
			dubois_botanical_expedition_possible_congo = yes
			NOR = {
				has_modifier = dubois_botanical_expedition_modifier
				has_modifier = dubois_naturalist_travell_to_location_modifier
				has_modifier = dubois_naturalist_travell_from_location_modifier
			}
			scope:dubois_naturalist_scope = {
				is_busy = no
			}
		}
		scope:dubois_naturalist_scope = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
		dubois_set_naturalist_to_congo = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = dubois_botanical_expedition_modifier
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = dubois_botanical_expedition_cost_modifier
			multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_very_small
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = dubois_naturalist_travell_to_location_modifier
			days = 90
		}
	}

	option = {	#To Borneo
		name = dubois.301.i
		trigger = {
			dubois_botanical_expedition_possible_borneo = yes
			NOR = {
				has_modifier = dubois_botanical_expedition_modifier
				has_modifier = dubois_naturalist_travell_to_location_modifier
				has_modifier = dubois_naturalist_travell_from_location_modifier
			}
			scope:dubois_naturalist_scope = {
				is_busy = no
			}
		}
		scope:dubois_naturalist_scope = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
		dubois_set_naturalist_to_borneo = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = dubois_botanical_expedition_modifier
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = dubois_botanical_expedition_cost_modifier
			multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_very_small
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = dubois_naturalist_travell_to_location_modifier
			days = 90
		}
	}

	option = {	#To Indochina
		name = dubois.301.j
		trigger = {
			dubois_botanical_expedition_possible_indochina = yes
			NOR = {
				has_modifier = dubois_botanical_expedition_modifier
				has_modifier = dubois_naturalist_travell_to_location_modifier
				has_modifier = dubois_naturalist_travell_from_location_modifier
			}
			scope:dubois_naturalist_scope = {
				is_busy = no
			}
		}
		scope:dubois_naturalist_scope = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
		dubois_set_naturalist_to_indochina = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = dubois_botanical_expedition_modifier
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = dubois_botanical_expedition_cost_modifier
			multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_very_small
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = dubois_naturalist_travell_to_location_modifier
			days = 90
		}
	}

	option = {	#Nevermind
		name = dubois.201.g
		default_option = yes
	}

	after = {
		remove_variable = dubois_paleontological_expedition_destination_selection_var
	}
}

#Dubois 302: Victoria amazonica (Amazonia)

dubois.302 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.302.t
	desc = dubois.302.d
	flavor = dubois.302.f

	placement = scope:dubois_botany_state

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_specimen_flower.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_botany.dds"

	cooldown = { 
		years = 10
	}

	trigger = {
		dubois_botanical_research = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		dubois_set_naturalist_location = yes
		var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
			save_scope_as = dubois_naturalist_scope
			set_variable = dubois_naturalist_found_victoria_amazonica_var
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.302.g #
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_type = building_dubois_zoo
				has_active_production_method = pm_botanical_garden
			}
			NOT = {
				any_scope_building = {
					has_modifier = dubois_victoria_amazonica_modifier
				}
			}
		}
		random_scope_building = {
			limit = {
				is_building_type = building_dubois_zoo
				has_active_production_method = pm_botanical_garden
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_victoria_amazonica_modifier
			}
		}
		naturalist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "10"
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.302.h #
		naturalist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "15"
		}
		dubois_small_add_technology = yes
		dubois_add_x_specimen_effect = { AMOUNT = 3000 }
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Dubois 309: IG questions botanical expedition

dubois.309 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.309.t
	desc = dubois.309.d
	flavor = dubois.309.f

	placement = scope:dubois_botany_state

	duration = 3

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:dubois_sceptical_leader

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_botany.dds"

	cooldown = { 
		years = 10
	}

	trigger = {
		dubois_botanical_research = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
			save_scope_as = dubois_naturalist_scope
		}
		random_interest_group = {
			limit = {
    			is_in_government = no
	        }
			save_scope_as = dubois_sceptical_ig
			leader = {
				save_scope_as = dubois_sceptical_leader
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.309.g #NATURALIST is scheduled to return immediately
		scope:dubois_sceptical_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = ig_placated
				years = 3
			}
		}
		scope:dubois_naturalist_scope = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = no
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_botany_banned_modifier
				years = 3
			}
		}
		dubois_set_naturalist_to_default = yes
		remove_modifier = dubois_botanical_expedition_modifier
		add_modifier = {
			name = dubois_naturalist_travell_from_location_modifier
			days = 90
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.309.h #We will not make science a political issue.
		default_option = yes
		dubois_add_x_specimen_effect = { AMOUNT = 3000 }
		scope:dubois_sceptical_ig  = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = ig_not_placated
				years = 3
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Dubois 411: Choose General

dubois.411 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.411.t
	desc = dubois.411.d
	flavor = dubois.411.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_mountaineering_beginning.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_geology.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_role = general
				is_busy = no
				OR = {
					has_trait = dubois_mountaineer
					has_trait = explorer
					has_trait = mountain_commander
					has_trait = surveyor
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_1
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_role = general
				is_busy = no
				OR = {
					has_trait = dubois_mountaineer
					has_trait = explorer
					has_trait = mountain_commander
					has_trait = surveyor
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_1
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_2
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_role = general
				is_busy = no
				OR = {
					has_trait = dubois_mountaineer
					has_trait = explorer
					has_trait = mountain_commander
					has_trait = surveyor
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_1
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_2
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_3
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.411.g #
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_1
		}
		scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_1 = {
			set_variable = dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_var
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_modifier = dubois_aspiring_climber_modifier
					}
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = dubois_aspiring_climber_modifier
					years = 10
				}
			}
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.411.h #
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_2
		}
		scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_2 = {
			set_variable = dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_var
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_modifier = dubois_aspiring_climber_modifier
					}
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = dubois_aspiring_climber_modifier
					years = 10
				}
			}
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.411.i #
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_3
		}
		scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_3 = {
			set_variable = dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_var
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_modifier = dubois_aspiring_climber_modifier
					}
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = dubois_aspiring_climber_modifier
					years = 10
				}
			}
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
	}

	after = {
		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.412
			days = { 7 10 }
		}
	}
}

#Dubois 412: Choose Mountain

dubois.412 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.412.t
	desc = dubois.412.d
	flavor = dubois.412.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_mountaineering_beginning.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_geology.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		set_dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_effect = yes
		random_state = {
			limit = {
				dubois_state_has_unconquered_summit = yes
				OR = {
					owner = ROOT
					owner = {
						has_diplomatic_pact = {
							who = ROOT
							type = mountaineering_license
						}
					}
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = dubois_summit_1
		}
		random_state = {
			limit = {
				dubois_state_has_unconquered_summit = yes
				OR = {
					owner = ROOT
					owner = {
						has_diplomatic_pact = {
							who = ROOT
							type = mountaineering_license
						}
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:dubois_summit_1
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = dubois_summit_2
		}
		random_state = {
			limit = {
				dubois_state_has_unconquered_summit = yes
				OR = {
					owner = ROOT
					owner = {
						has_diplomatic_pact = {
							who = ROOT
							type = mountaineering_license
						}
					}
				}
				NOR = {
					this = scope:dubois_summit_1
					this = scope:dubois_summit_2
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = dubois_summit_3
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.412.g #Mountain State 1
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:dubois_summit_1
		}
		scope:dubois_summit_1 = {
			set_variable = dubois_targeted_summit_var
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.412.h #Mountain State 2
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:dubois_summit_2
		}
		scope:dubois_summit_2 = {
			set_variable = dubois_targeted_summit_var
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.412.i #Mountain State 3
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:dubois_summit_3
		}
		scope:dubois_summit_3 = {
			set_variable = dubois_targeted_summit_var
		}
	}

	after = {
		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.413
			days = { 7 10 }
		}
		set_dubois_mountain_choice_effect = yes
	}
}

#Dubois 413: Associate Scientist

dubois.413 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.413.t
	desc = dubois.413.d
	flavor = dubois.413.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_mountaineering_beginning.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_geology.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		set_dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_effect = yes
		set_dubois_summit_location = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dubois_naturalist_var
			}
			var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
				save_scope_as = dubois_naturalist_scope
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_var
			}
			var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
				save_scope_as = dubois_paleontologist_scope
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dubois_geologist_var
			}
			var:dubois_geologist_var = {
				save_scope_as = dubois_geologist_scope
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.413.g #There is no need for a scientist
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.413.h #A Geologist
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:dubois_geologist_scope
			scope:dubois_geologist_scope = {
				is_busy = no
			}
		}
		scope:dubois_geologist_scope = {
			set_variable = dubois_mountain_scientist_var
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.413.i #A Naturalist
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:dubois_naturalist_scope
			scope:dubois_naturalist_scope = {
				is_busy = no
			}
		}
		scope:dubois_naturalist_scope = {
			set_variable = dubois_mountain_scientist_var
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.413.j #A Paleontologist
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope
			scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope = {
				is_busy = no
			}
		}
		scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope = {
			set_variable = dubois_mountain_scientist_var
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
	}

	after = {
		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.414
			days = { 21 31 }
		}
	}
}

#Dubois 414: Mountain Expedition starts

dubois.414 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.414.t
	desc = dubois.414.d
	flavor = dubois.414.f

	placement = scope:dubois_summit_location

	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_mountaineering_beginning.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_geology.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		set_dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_effect = yes
		set_dubois_summit_location = yes
		set_dubois_mountain_expedition_scientist_effect = yes
		set_dubois_mountain_climbing_progress = yes
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_variable = dubois_mountain_ascents_var } }
			set_variable = {
				name = dubois_mountain_ascents_var
				value = 1
			}
		}
		else = {
			change_variable = {
				name = dubois_mountain_ascents_var
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.414.g #The mountain calls
		default_option = yes
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = je_dubois_mountain_expedition
		}
	}
}

###Mountaineering Expedition End###

#Dubois 420: The Summit

dubois.420 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.420.t
	desc = dubois.420.d
	flavor = dubois.420.f

	placement = scope:dubois_summit_location

	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_mountaineering_summit.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_geology.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		set_dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_effect = yes
		set_dubois_summit_location = yes
		set_dubois_mountain_expedition_scientist_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.420.g #Let's enjoy the dawn!
		default_option = yes
		set_dubois_summit_reached_effect = yes
		set_dubois_promote_mountain_expedition_leader_effect = yes
		add_dubois_mountain_expedition_prestige_bonus = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = scope:dubois_mountain_scientist
			}
			add_dubois_mountain_expedition_science_bonus = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
						has_trait = dubois_mountaineer
						has_trait = explorer
						has_trait = mountain_commander
					}
					NOR = {
						has_modifier = dubois_mountaineering_regiment_modifier
						has_modifier = dubois_summit_level_1_modifier # You don't get Alpini or Gebirsgjäger when climbing a mere hill!
					}
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = dubois.423
					days = { 30 50 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						elgar_has_great_composer = yes
						elgar_has_composer = yes
					}
					NOR = {
						has_variable = elgar_alpine_symphony_var
						has_modifier = dubois_summit_level_1_modifier # You don't get an Alpine Symphony when climbing a mere hill!
					}
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = dubois.424
					days = { 7 14 }
				}
			}
		}	
	}

	after = {
		remove_dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_effect = yes
		remove_dubois_mountain_expedition_scientist_effect = yes
		remove_dubois_mountain_choice_effect = yes
	}
}

#Dubois 421: Mountaineering Disaster

dubois.421 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.421.t
	desc = dubois.421.d
	flavor = dubois.421.f

	placement = scope:dubois_summit_location

	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_mountaineering_disaster.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_geology.dds"

	trigger = {
		NOR = {
			has_modifier = dubois_mountaineering_disaster_modifier
			has_modifier = dubois_mountaineering_disappointment_modifier
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_effect = yes
		set_dubois_summit_location = yes
		set_dubois_mountain_expedition_scientist_effect = yes
		set_variable = {
			name = dubois_mountain_expedition_fail
			months = 1
		}
		

		ig:ig_armed_forces = {
			save_scope_as = army_ig
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_variable = dubois_mountain_disasters_var } }
			set_variable = {
				name = dubois_mountain_disasters_var
				value = 1
			}
		}
		else = {
			change_variable = {
				name = dubois_mountain_disasters_var
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.421.g #Horrendeous!
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = dubois_mountaineering_disaster_modifier
			years = 5
		}
		scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
			add_trait = wounded
			remove_modifier = dubois_aspiring_climber_modifier
		}
		scope:dubois_summit_location = {
			add_modifier = dubois_death_peak_modifier
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					scope:dubois_summit_location = {
						has_modifier = dubois_first_ascent_modifier
					}
					scope:dubois_summit_location = {
						has_modifier = dubois_death_peak_modifier
					}
				}
			}
			scope:dubois_summit_location = {
				add_modifier = dubois_death_peak_modifier
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			random_list = {
				75 = {}
				20 = {
					scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
						add_trait = psychological_affliction
					}
				}
				5 = {
					scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
						kill_character = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		scope:army_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = lepsius_insulted_military_modifier
				years = 1
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		remove_dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_effect = yes
		remove_dubois_mountain_expedition_scientist_effect = yes
		remove_dubois_mountain_choice_effect = yes
	}
}

#Dubois 422: Climb aborted

dubois.422 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.422.t
	desc = dubois.422.d
	flavor = dubois.422.f

	placement = scope:dubois_summit_location

	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_mountaineering_beginning.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_geology.dds"

	trigger = {
		NOR = {
			has_modifier = dubois_mountaineering_disaster_modifier
			has_modifier = dubois_mountaineering_disappointment_modifier
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_effect = yes
		set_dubois_summit_location = yes
		set_dubois_mountain_expedition_scientist_effect = yes
		set_variable = {
			name = dubois_mountain_expedition_fail
			months = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_variable = dubois_mountain_climbs_aborted_var } }
			set_variable = {
				name = dubois_mountain_climbs_aborted_var
				value = 1
			}
		}
		else = {
			change_variable = {
				name = dubois_mountain_climbs_aborted_var
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.422.g #Disappointing
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = dubois_mountaineering_disappointment_modifier
			years = 3
		}
	}

	after = {
		remove_dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_effect = yes
		remove_dubois_mountain_expedition_scientist_effect = yes
		remove_dubois_mountain_choice_effect = yes
	}
}

dubois.423 = {

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_music.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = dubois_mountaineer
				has_trait = explorer
				has_trait = mountain_commander
			}
			save_scope_as = dubois_mountain_veteran
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.423.g #They will carry his legacy into the future.
		add_modifier = {
			name = dubois_mountaineering_regiment_modifier
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Dubois 430: An Easy Climb

dubois.430 = {
	type = country_event

	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_geology.dds"

	cooldown = {
		days = 60
	}

	trigger = {
		var:dubois_mountain_climbing_progress <= 3
	}

	immediate = {
		set_dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_effect = yes
		set_dubois_summit_location = yes
		set_dubois_mountain_expedition_scientist_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.430.g #Go ahead!
		add_dubois_mountain_climbing_progress = yes
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Dubois 431: A Slope

dubois.431 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.431.t
	desc = dubois.431.d
	flavor = dubois.431.f

	placement = scope:dubois_summit_location

	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_mountaineering_climb.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_geology.dds"

	cooldown = {
		days = 60
	}

	trigger = {
		var:dubois_mountain_climbing_progress <= 4
	}

	immediate = {
		set_dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_effect = yes
		set_dubois_summit_location = yes
		set_dubois_mountain_expedition_scientist_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.431.g #We will master this
		default_option = yes
		random_list = {
			35 = {
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = opium_addiction
									has_trait = senile
									has_trait = wounded
									has_trait = psychological_affliction
								}
							}
						}
						add = 15
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = wrathful
									has_trait = hedonist
									has_trait = plains_commander
								}
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								age >= 65
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								age >= 75
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { 
					id = dubois.422 #Fail
					popup = yes
				}
			}
			65 = {
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = surveyor
							}
						}
						add = 5
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_modifier = dubois_aspiring_climber_modifier
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = cautious
									has_trait = meticulous
								}
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = brave
									has_trait = innovative
								}
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = ambitious
									has_trait = persistent
								}
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = explorer
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = mountain_commander
							}
						}
						add = 20
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = dubois_mountaineer
							}
						}
						add = 20
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							exists = scope:dubois_mountain_scientist
							scope:dubois_mountain_scientist = {
								has_trait = dubois_mountaineer
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
				}
				add_dubois_mountain_climbing_progress = yes #Success
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.431.h #This is too risky
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Dubois 432: Steep Wall

dubois.432 = {

									has_trait = innovative

#Dubois 433: Avalanche

dubois.433 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.433.t
	desc = dubois.433.d
	flavor = dubois.433.f

		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_mountaineering_climb.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_geology.dds"

	cooldown = {
		days = 120
	}

	trigger = {
		var:dubois_mountain_climbing_progress <= 6
		var:dubois_mountain_climbing_progress > 2
	}

	immediate = {
		set_dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_effect = yes
		set_dubois_summit_location = yes
		set_dubois_mountain_expedition_scientist_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.430.g #Go ahead
		random_list = {
			60 = {
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = opium_addiction
									has_trait = senile
									has_trait = wounded
									has_trait = psychological_affliction
								}
							}
						}
						add = 15
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = wrathful
									has_trait = hedonist
									has_trait = plains_commander
								}
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								age >= 65
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								age >= 75
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { 
					id = dubois.421 #Dangerous Fail
					popup = yes
				}

			40 = {

						limit = {

								has_trait = surveyor
							}

							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = cautious
									has_trait = meticulous
								}
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = brave
									has_trait = innovative
								}
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = ambitious
									has_trait = persistent
								}
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = explorer
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = mountain_commander
							}
						}
						add = 20
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = dubois_mountaineer
							}
						}
						add = 20
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							exists = scope:dubois_mountain_scientist
							scope:dubois_mountain_scientist = {
								has_trait = dubois_mountaineer
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
				}
				add_dubois_mountain_climbing_progress = yes #Success
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.431.h #This is too risky
		default_option = yes
		random_list = {
			65 = {}
			35 = {
				trigger_event = { 
					id = dubois.422 #Fail
					days = 3
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.433.h #Search another way
		sub_dubois_mountain_climbing_progress = yes
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Dubois 434: Abyss

dubois.434 = {
	type = country_event

	cooldown = {
		days = 60
	}

	trigger = {
		var:dubois_mountain_climbing_progress <= 7
		var:dubois_mountain_climbing_progress > 3
	}

	immediate = {
		set_dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_effect = yes
		set_dubois_summit_location = yes
		set_dubois_mountain_expedition_scientist_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.433.g #Go ahead
		random_list = {
			55 = {
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = opium_addiction
									has_trait = senile
									has_trait = wounded
									has_trait = psychological_affliction
								}
							}
						}
						add = 15
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = wrathful
									has_trait = hedonist
									has_trait = plains_commander
								}
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								age >= 65
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								age >= 75
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { 
					id = dubois.421 #Dangerous Fail
					popup = yes
				}
			}
			45 = {
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = surveyor
							}
						}
						add = 5
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_modifier = dubois_aspiring_climber_modifier
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = cautious
									has_trait = meticulous
								}
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = brave
									has_trait = innovative
								}
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = ambitious
									has_trait = persistent
								}
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = explorer
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = mountain_commander
							}
						}
						add = 20
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = dubois_mountaineer
							}
						}
						add = 20
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							exists = scope:dubois_mountain_scientist
							scope:dubois_mountain_scientist = {
								has_trait = dubois_mountaineer
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
				}
				add_dubois_mountain_climbing_progress = yes #Success
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.431.h #This is too risky
		default_option = yes
		random_list = {
			50 = {}
			50 = {
				trigger_event = { 
					id = dubois.422 #Fail
					days = 3
				}
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Dubois 435: Weather Change

dubois.435 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.435.t
	desc = dubois.435.d
	flavor = dubois.435.f

	placement = scope:dubois_summit_location

	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_mountaineering_climb.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_geology.dds"

	cooldown = {
		days = 60
	}

	trigger = {
		var:dubois_mountain_climbing_progress <= 7
		var:dubois_mountain_climbing_progress > 4
	}

	immediate = {
		set_dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_effect = yes
		set_dubois_summit_location = yes
		set_dubois_mountain_expedition_scientist_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.433.g #Go ahead
		random_list = {
			65 = {
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = opium_addiction
									has_trait = senile
									has_trait = wounded
									has_trait = psychological_affliction
								}
							}
						}
						add = 15
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = wrathful
									has_trait = hedonist
									has_trait = plains_commander
								}
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								age >= 65
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								age >= 75
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { 
					id = dubois.421 #Dangerous Fail
					popup = yes
				}
			}
			35 = {
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = surveyor
							}
						}
						add = 5
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_modifier = dubois_aspiring_climber_modifier
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = cautious
									has_trait = meticulous
								}
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = brave
									has_trait = innovative
								}
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = ambitious
									has_trait = persistent
								}
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = explorer
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = mountain_commander
							}
						}
						add = 20
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = dubois_mountaineer
							}
						}
						add = 20
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							exists = scope:dubois_mountain_scientist
							scope:dubois_mountain_scientist = {
								has_trait = dubois_mountaineer
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
				}
				add_dubois_mountain_climbing_progress = yes #Success
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.435.h #Back to the last base camp!
		default_option = yes
		sub_dubois_mountain_climbing_progress = yes
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Dubois 436: Death Step

dubois.436 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.436.t
	desc = dubois.436.d
	flavor = dubois.436.f

	placement = scope:dubois_summit_location

	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_mountaineering_climb.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_geology.dds"

	cooldown = {
		days = 120
	}

	trigger = {
		var:dubois_mountain_climbing_progress <= 7
		var:dubois_mountain_climbing_progress > 5
	}

	immediate = {
		set_dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_effect = yes
		set_dubois_summit_location = yes
		set_dubois_mountain_expedition_scientist_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.433.g #Go ahead
		random_list = {
			70 = {
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = opium_addiction
									has_trait = senile
									has_trait = wounded
									has_trait = psychological_affliction
								}
							}
						}
						add = 15
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = wrathful
									has_trait = hedonist
									has_trait = plains_commander
								}
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								age >= 65
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								age >= 75
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { 
					id = dubois.421 #Dangerous Fail
					popup = yes
				}
			}
			30 = {
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = surveyor
							}
						}
						add = 5
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_modifier = dubois_aspiring_climber_modifier
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = cautious
									has_trait = meticulous
								}
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = brave
									has_trait = innovative
								}
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = ambitious
									has_trait = persistent
								}
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = explorer
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = mountain_commander
							}
						}
						add = 20
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = dubois_mountaineer
							}
						}
						add = 20
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							exists = scope:dubois_mountain_scientist
							scope:dubois_mountain_scientist = {
								has_trait = dubois_mountaineer
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
				}
				add_dubois_mountain_climbing_progress = yes #Success
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.433.h #There must be an alternative route!
		default_option = yes
		random_list = {
			60 = {
				modifier = {
					if = {

								OR = {
									has_trait = opium_addiction
									has_trait = senile

									has_trait = psychological_affliction

							}

					}

									has_trait = cautious

							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = brave

									has_trait = ambitious
									has_trait = persistent

							}

					}

						add = 10
					}

				sub_dubois_mountain_climbing_progress = yes #"Success"
