						add = 5
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_modifier = dubois_aspiring_climber_modifier
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = cautious
									has_trait = meticulous
								}
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = brave
									has_trait = innovative
								}
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = ambitious
									has_trait = persistent
								}
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = explorer
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = mountain_commander
							}
						}
						add = 20
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = dubois_mountaineer
							}
						}
						add = 20
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							exists = scope:dubois_mountain_scientist
							scope:dubois_mountain_scientist = {
								has_trait = dubois_mountaineer
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
				}
				add_dubois_mountain_climbing_progress = yes #Success
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.438.g #Good that we have modern medical equipment.
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			has_technology_researched = triage
		}
		add_dubois_mountain_climbing_progress = yes #Success
		custom_tooltip = dubois_triage_tt
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.438.h #We wait until they recover
		sub_dubois_mountain_climbing_progress = yes #Success
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Dubois 439: Rope Group

dubois.439 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.439.t
	desc = dubois.439.d
	flavor = dubois.439.f

	placement = scope:dubois_summit_location

	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_mountaineering_climb.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_geology.dds"

	cooldown = {
		years = 1
	}

	trigger = {
		var:dubois_mountain_climbing_progress <= 5
		var:dubois_mountain_climbing_progress > 1
	}

	immediate = {
		set_dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_effect = yes
		set_dubois_summit_location = yes
		set_dubois_mountain_expedition_scientist_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.433.g #Go ahead
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = opium_addiction
									has_trait = senile
									has_trait = wounded
									has_trait = psychological_affliction
								}
							}
						}
						add = 15
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = wrathful
									has_trait = hedonist
									has_trait = plains_commander
								}
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								age >= 65
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								age >= 75
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { 
					id = dubois.421 #Dangerous Fail
					popup = yes
				}
			}
			50 = {
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = surveyor
							}
						}
						add = 5
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_modifier = dubois_aspiring_climber_modifier
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = cautious
									has_trait = meticulous
								}
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = brave
									has_trait = innovative
								}
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = ambitious
									has_trait = persistent
								}
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = explorer
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = mountain_commander
							}
						}
						add = 20
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = dubois_mountaineer
							}
						}
						add = 20
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							exists = scope:dubois_mountain_scientist
							scope:dubois_mountain_scientist = {
								has_trait = dubois_mountaineer
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
				}
				add_dubois_mountain_climbing_progress = yes #Success
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.438.g #Good that we have modern organization.
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			has_technology_researched = logistics
		}
		add_dubois_mountain_climbing_progress = yes #Success
		custom_tooltip = dubois_logistics_tt
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.431.h #This is too risky
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Dubois 440: Scientist does Science

dubois.440 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.440.t
	desc = dubois.440.d
	flavor = dubois.440.f

	placement = scope:dubois_summit_location

	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_mountaineering_scientist.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_geology.dds"

	cooldown = {
		days = 100
	}

	trigger = {
		exists = scope:dubois_mountain_scientist
	}

	immediate = {
		set_dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_effect = yes
		set_dubois_summit_location = yes
		set_dubois_mountain_expedition_scientist_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.440.g #Congratulations
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dubois_naturalist_var
				var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
					has_variable = dubois_mountain_scientist_var
				}
			}
			dubois_add_x_specimen_effect = { AMOUNT = 1000 }
			naturalist_experience_gain_effect = {
				AMOUNT = "5"
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_var
				var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
					has_variable = dubois_mountain_scientist_var
				}
			}
			dubois_add_x_fossils_effect = { AMOUNT = 1 }
			paleontologist_experience_gain_effect = {
				AMOUNT = "5"
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

			has_variable = dubois_mountain_scientist_var

		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.148
				days = { 30 60 }
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Dubois 901: Hippocampus - Invitation

dubois.901 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.901.t
	desc = dubois.901.d
	flavor = dubois.901.f

	duration = 1

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_hippocampus_congress.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = dubois_unique_yes
		set_global_variable = dubois_unique_no
		var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
			set_variable = dubois_attended_hippocampus_congress_var
			save_scope_as = dubois_naturalist_scope
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
					has_variable = dubois_invented_evolution_theory_var
				}
			}
			var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
				save_scope_as = dubois_darwin_scope
			}
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = dubois.901.g # Invite the leading naturalist nations
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					this = ROOT 
				}
				has_variable = dubois_naturalist_var
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.902
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.904
			days = { 7 14 }
		}
		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.909
			days = 180
		}
	}
}

#Dubois 904: Hippocampus - Relation to Ape or Uniqueness?

dubois.904 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.904.t
	desc = dubois.904.d
	flavor = dubois.904.f

	duration = 2

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_hippocampus_congress.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	immediate = {
		var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
			save_scope_as = dubois_naturalist_scope
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dubois_naturalist_var
				NOT = {
					this = ROOT
				}
			}
			var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
				save_scope_as = dubois_hippocampus_defender_scope
			}
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dubois_naturalist_var
				NOT = {
					this = ROOT
				}
				var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
					NOT = {
						this = scope:dubois_hippocampus_defender_scope
					}
				}
			}
			var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
				save_scope_as = dubois_hippocampus_attacker_scope
			}
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = dubois.904.g #Man is unique in the animal kingdom
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
					has_trait = dubois_naturalist_famous
				}
			}
			change_global_variable = {
				name = dubois_unique_yes
				add = 3
			}
			custom_tooltip = dubois_conference_naturalist_triple_vote_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
					has_trait = dubois_naturalist_experienced
				}
			}
			change_global_variable = {
				name = dubois_unique_yes
				add = 2
			}
			custom_tooltip = dubois_conference_naturalist_double_vote_tt
		}
		else = {
			change_global_variable = {
				name = dubois_unique_yes
				add = 1
			}
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = { #State Church
				trigger = {
					has_law = law_type:law_state_religion
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #Powerful Clergy
				trigger = {
					ig:ig_devout = {
						is_powerful = yes
					}
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #Cautious Character preserves status quo
				trigger = {
					var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
						has_trait = cautious
					}
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #Less experiences remains conformist
				trigger = {
					var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
						var:dubois_naturalist_experience < 100
					}
				}
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = dubois.904.h #Man is nearer to apes than we thought before
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
					has_trait = dubois_naturalist_famous
				}
			}
			change_global_variable = {
				name = dubois_unique_no
				add = 3
			}
			custom_tooltip = dubois_conference_naturalist_triple_vote_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
					has_trait = dubois_naturalist_experienced
				}
			}
			change_global_variable = {
				name = dubois_unique_no
				add = 2
			}
			custom_tooltip = dubois_conference_naturalist_double_vote_tt
		}
		else = {
			change_global_variable = {
				name = dubois_unique_no
				add = 1
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = { #Total Seperation or Atheism
				trigger = {
					OR = {
						has_law = law_type:law_total_separation
						has_law = law_type:law_state_atheism
					}
				}
				add = 1
			}	
			modifier = { #Atheist Archaeologist
				trigger = {
					var:lepsius_archaeologist_var = {
						has_ideology = ideology:ideology_anti_clerical
					}
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #Powerless Clergy
				trigger = {
					ig:ig_devout = {
						is_marginal = yes
					}
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #Theory of Evolution will help significantly
				trigger = {
					has_technology_researched = dubois_theory_of_evolution_tech
				}
				add = 5
			}
			modifier = { #Innovative will tend to Theory of Evolution
				trigger = {
					var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
						has_trait = innovative
					}
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #More experience ist non-conformist
				trigger = {
					var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
						var:dubois_naturalist_experience >= 100
					}
				}
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = { #Mr. Darwin will defend his theory at all cost
				trigger = {
					var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
						has_variable = dubois_invented_evolution_theory_var
					}
				}
				add = 20
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = inspirational_orator
						has_trait = demagogue
						has_trait = firebrand
						has_trait = charismatic
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.905 #Respected Speech
				days = { 14 21 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = innovative
						has_trait = meticulous
						has_trait = erudite
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.906 #Valuable contribution to the debate
				days = { 14 21 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_character = {
					has_trait = literary
				}
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.907 #The Hippopotamus
				days = { 14 21 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.908 #Intellectural or material exchange
				days = { 14 21 }
			}
		}
	}
}

#Dubois 905: Hippocampus - Respected Speech

dubois.905 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.905.t
	desc = dubois.905.d
	flavor = dubois.905.f

	duration = 1

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_hippocampus_congress.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = dubois_congress_host_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = dubois_congress_host_country
		}
		var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
			save_scope_as = dubois_naturalist_scope
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					this = ROOT
				}
				OR = {
					has_modifier = dubois_congress_host_modifier
					has_modifier = dubois_congress_attend_modifier
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = dubois_congress_country
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = dubois.905.g #He brings honor to our country
		dubois_add_x_academy_progress = {
			AMOUNT = "3"
		}
		change_infamy = -3
		scope:dubois_congress_country = {
			change_relations = {
				country = ROOT 
				value = 10
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = innovative
						has_trait = meticulous
						has_trait = erudite
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.906 #Valuable contribution to the debate
				days = { 14 21 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_character = {
					has_trait = literary
				}
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.907 #The Hippopotamus
				days = { 14 21 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.908 #Intellectural or material exchange
				days = { 14 21 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	immediate = {

			limit = {
				has_modifier = dubois_congress_host_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = dubois_congress_host_country
		}
		var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
			save_scope_as = dubois_naturalist_scope
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					this = ROOT
				}
				OR = {
					has_modifier = dubois_congress_host_modifier
					has_modifier = dubois_congress_attend_modifier
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = dubois_congress_country
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = dubois.905.g #He brings honor to our country

			change_relations = {
				country = ROOT 
				value = 10
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_character = {
					has_trait = literary
				}
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.907 #The Hippopotamus
				days = { 14 21 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.908 #Intellectural or material exchange
				days = { 14 21 }
			}
		}
	}

#Dubois 909: Hippocampus - Decision for Host

dubois.909 = {
	type = country_event

	title = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = dubois_hippocampus_unique
			}
			desc = dubois.909.t_unique
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = dubois_hippocampus_primate
			}
			desc = dubois.909.t_primate
		}
	}

	desc = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = dubois_hippocampus_unique
			}
			desc = dubois.909.d_unique
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = dubois_hippocampus_primate
			}
			desc = dubois.909.d_primate
		}
	}

	flavor = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = dubois_hippocampus_unique
			}
			desc = dubois.909.f_unique
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = dubois_hippocampus_primate
			}
			desc = dubois.909.f_primate
		}
	}

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_hippocampus_congress.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = dubois_congress_host_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = dubois_congress_host_country
		}
		var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
			save_scope_as = dubois_naturalist_scope
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				global_var:dubois_unique_yes > global_var:dubois_unique_no
			}
			set_global_variable = dubois_hippocampus_unique
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				global_var:dubois_unique_yes = global_var:dubois_unique_no
			}
			set_global_variable = dubois_hippocampus_primate
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				global_var:dubois_unique_yes < global_var:dubois_unique_no
			}
			set_global_variable = dubois_hippocampus_primate
		}
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_global_variable = dubois_hippocampus_unique
		}
		name = dubois.909.g #Man is the crown of creation.
		default_option = yes
		dubois_small_add_technology = yes
		naturalist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "10"
		}
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_global_variable = dubois_hippocampus_primate
		}
		name = dubois.909.h #Are we just hairless monkeys?
		dubois_large_add_technology = yes
		naturalist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "20"
		}
	}

	after = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					this = ROOT 
				}
				has_modifier = dubois_congress_attend_modifier
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.910
				popup = yes
			}
		}
		remove_global_variable = dubois_unique_yes
		remove_global_variable = dubois_unique_no
	}
}

#Dubois 911: Origin - Invitation

dubois.911 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.911.t
	desc = dubois.911.d
	flavor = dubois.911.f

	duration = 1

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_origin_congress.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_anthropology.dds"

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = dubois_origin_europe
		set_global_variable = dubois_origin_asia
		set_global_variable = dubois_origin_africa
		var:lepsius_anthropologist_var = {
			set_variable = dubois_attended_origin_congress_var
			save_scope_as = lepsius_anthropologist_scope
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = dubois.911.g # Invite the leading anthropologist nations
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					this = ROOT 
				}
				has_variable = lepsius_anthropologist_var
				OR = {
					var:lepsius_neanderthalensis_human_fossil >= 1
					var:lepsius_erectus_human_fossil >= 1
					var:lepsius_australopithecus_human_fossil >= 1
					var:lepsius_paranthropus_human_fossil >= 1
				}
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.912
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.914
			days = { 7 14 }
		}
		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.919
			days = 180
		}
	}
}

#Dubois 914: Origin - Europe, Asia or Africa?

dubois.914 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.914.t
	desc = dubois.914.d
	flavor = dubois.914.f

	duration = 2

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_origin_congress.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_anthropology.dds"

	immediate = {
		var:lepsius_anthropologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = lepsius_anthropologist_scope
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_anthropologist_var
				NOT = {
					this = ROOT
				}
			}
			var:lepsius_anthropologist_var = {
				save_scope_as = dubois_asia_defender_scope
			}
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_anthropologist_var
				NOT = {
					this = ROOT
				}
				var:lepsius_anthropologist_var = {
					NOT = {
						this = scope:dubois_africa_defender_scope
					}
				}
			}
			var:lepsius_anthropologist_var = {
				save_scope_as = dubois_africa_defender_scope
			}
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lepsius_anthropologist_var
				NOT = {
					this = ROOT
				}
				var:lepsius_anthropologist_var = {
					NOT = {
						this = scope:dubois_asia_defender_scope
					}
					NOT = {
						this = scope:dubois_africa_defender_scope
					}
				}
			}
			var:lepsius_anthropologist_var = {
				save_scope_as = dubois_europe_defender_scope
			}
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = dubois.914.g #Europe
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_anthropologist_var = {
					has_trait = lepsius_anthropologist_famous
				}
			}
			change_global_variable = {
				name = dubois_origin_europe
				add = 3
			}
			custom_tooltip = dubois_conference_anthropologist_double_vote_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_anthropologist_var = {
					has_trait = lepsius_anthropologist_experienced
				}
			}
			change_global_variable = {
				name = dubois_origin_europe
				add = 2
			}
			custom_tooltip = dubois_conference_anthropologist_triple_vote_tt
		}
		else = {
			change_global_variable = {
				name = dubois_origin_europe
				add = 1
			}
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = { #No Erectus
				trigger = {
					NOT = {
						has_variable = lepsius_erectus_human_fossil
					}
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #No Australopithecus or Paranthropus
				trigger = {
					NOR = {
						has_variable = lepsius_australopithecus_human_fossil
						has_variable = lepsius_paranthropus_human_fossil
					}
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #No Systemization
				trigger = {
					NOR = {
						has_global_variable = lepsius_erectus_systemized
						has_global_variable = lepsius_australopithecus_systemized
						has_global_variable = lepsius_paranthropus_systemized
					}
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #Piltdown Man
				trigger = {
					has_variable = dubois_fossil_piltdown
				}
				add = 10
			}
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = dubois.914.h #Asia
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_anthropologist_var = {
					has_trait = lepsius_anthropologist_famous
				}
			}
			change_global_variable = {
				name = dubois_origin_asia
				add = 3
			}
			custom_tooltip = dubois_conference_anthropologist_double_vote_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_anthropologist_var = {
					has_trait = lepsius_anthropologist_experienced
				}
			}
			change_global_variable = {
				name = dubois_origin_asia
				add = 2
			}
			custom_tooltip = dubois_conference_anthropologist_triple_vote_tt
		}
		else = {
			change_global_variable = {
				name = dubois_origin_asia
				add = 1
			}
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = { #Erectus
				trigger = {
					has_variable = lepsius_erectus_human_fossil
				}
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = { #No Australopithecus or Paranthropus
				trigger = {
					NOR = {
						has_variable = lepsius_australopithecus_human_fossil
						has_variable = lepsius_paranthropus_human_fossil
					}
				}
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = { #Erectus Systemization
				trigger = {
					has_global_variable = lepsius_erectus_systemized
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #No Australopithecus or Paranthropus Systemization
				trigger = {
					NOR = {
						has_global_variable = lepsius_australopithecus_systemized
						has_global_variable = lepsius_paranthropus_systemized
					}
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #Genetics
				trigger = {
					has_technology_researched = dubois_genetics_tech
				}
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = dubois.914.i #Africa
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_anthropologist_var = {
					has_trait = lepsius_anthropologist_famous
				}
			}
			change_global_variable = {
				name = dubois_origin_africa
				add = 3
			}
			custom_tooltip = dubois_conference_anthropologist_double_vote_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_anthropologist_var = {
					has_trait = lepsius_anthropologist_experienced
				}
			}
			change_global_variable = {
				name = dubois_origin_africa
				add = 2
			}
			custom_tooltip = dubois_conference_anthropologist_triple_vote_tt
		}
		else = {
			change_global_variable = {
				name = dubois_origin_africa
				add = 1
			}
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = { #Erectus
				trigger = {
					has_variable = lepsius_erectus_human_fossil
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #Australopithecus
				trigger = {
					has_variable = lepsius_australopithecus_human_fossil
				}
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = { #No Australopithecus or Paranthropus
				trigger = {
					has_variable = lepsius_paranthropus_human_fossil
				}
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = { #Erectus Systemization
				trigger = {
					has_global_variable = lepsius_erectus_systemized
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #Australopithecus Systemization
				trigger = {
					has_global_variable = lepsius_australopithecus_systemized
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #Paranthropus Systemization
				trigger = {
					has_global_variable = lepsius_paranthropus_systemized
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = { #Genetics
				trigger = {
					has_technology_researched = dubois_genetics_tech
				}
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}

	

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_anthropologist_var = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = inspirational_orator
						has_trait = demagogue
						has_trait = firebrand
						has_trait = charismatic
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.915 #Respected Speech
				days = { 14 21 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_anthropologist_var = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = innovative
						has_trait = meticulous
						has_trait = erudite
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.916 #Valuable contribution to the debate
				days = { 14 21 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.917 #Unknown Skull
				days = { 14 21 }
			}
		}
	}
}

dubois.915 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.915.t
	desc = dubois.915.d
	flavor = dubois.915.f

	duration = 1

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_origin_congress.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_anthropology.dds"

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = dubois_congress_host_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = dubois_congress_host_country
		}
		var:lepsius_anthropologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = lepsius_anthropologist_scope
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					this = ROOT
				}
				OR = {
					has_modifier = dubois_congress_host_modifier
					has_modifier = dubois_congress_attend_modifier
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = dubois_congress_country
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = dubois.905.g #He brings honor to our country
		dubois_add_x_academy_progress = {
			AMOUNT = "3"
		}
		change_infamy = -3
		scope:dubois_congress_country = {
			change_relations = {
				country = ROOT 
				value = 10
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:lepsius_anthropologist_var = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = innovative
						has_trait = meticulous
						has_trait = erudite
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.916 #Valuable contribution to the debate
				days = { 14 21 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.917 #Unknown Skull
				days = { 14 21 }
			}
		}
	}
}

#Dubois 917: Origin - Unknown Skull

dubois.917 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.917.t
	desc = dubois.917.d
	flavor = dubois.917.f

	duration = 1

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_origin_congress.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_anthropology.dds"

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = dubois_congress_host_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = dubois_congress_host_country
		}
		var:lepsius_anthropologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = lepsius_anthropologist_scope
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					this = ROOT
				}
				OR = {
					has_modifier = dubois_congress_host_modifier
					has_modifier = dubois_congress_attend_modifier
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = dubois_congress_country
		}
		random_list = { #randomizes skull
			1 = { 
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_cromagnon_skull_var
					value = 1
				}
			}
			1 = { 
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_neanderthalensis_skull_var
					value = 2
				}
			}
			1 = { 
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_erectus_skull_var
					value = 3
				}
			}
			1 = { 
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_australopithecus_skull_var
					value = 4
				}
			}
			1 = { 
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_paranthropus_skull_var
					value = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = dubois.917.g #Buy the skull
		default_option = yes
		add_treasury = -100000
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dubois_cromagnon_skull_var
			}
			lepsius_add_unknown_cromagnon_fossil_effect = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dubois_neanderthalensis_skull_var
			}
			lepsius_add_unknown_neanderthalensis_fossil_effect = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dubois_erectus_skull_var
			}
			lepsius_add_unknown_erectus_fossil_effect = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dubois_australopithecus_skull_var
			}
			lepsius_add_unknown_australopithecus_fossil_effect = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dubois_paranthropus_skull_var
			}
			lepsius_add_unknown_paranthropus_fossil_effect = yes
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = dubois.917.h #This is a fake
	}

	after = {
		remove_variable = dubois_cromagnon_skull_var
		remove_variable = dubois_neanderthalensis_skull_var
		remove_variable = dubois_erectus_skull_var
		remove_variable = dubois_australopithecus_skull_var
		remove_variable = dubois_paranthropus_skull_var
	}
}

#Dubois 919: Origin - Decision for Host

dubois.919 = {
	type = country_event

	title = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = dubois_origin_europe_vote
			}
			desc = dubois.919.t_europe
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = dubois_origin_asia_vote
			}
			desc = dubois.919.t_asia
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = dubois_origin_africa_vote
			}
			desc = dubois.919.t_africa
		}
	}

	desc = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = dubois_origin_europe_vote
			}
			desc = dubois.919.d_europe
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = dubois_origin_asia_vote
			}
			desc = dubois.919.d_asia
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = dubois_origin_africa_vote
			}
			desc = dubois.919.d_africa
		}
	}

	flavor = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = dubois_origin_europe_vote
			}
			desc = dubois.919.f_europe
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = dubois_origin_asia_vote
			}
			desc = dubois.919.f_asia
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = dubois_origin_africa_vote
			}
			desc = dubois.919.f_africa
		}
	}

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_origin_congress.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_anthropology.dds"

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = dubois_congress_host_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = dubois_congress_host_country
		}
		var:lepsius_anthropologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = lepsius_anthropologist_scope
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				global_var:dubois_origin_europe > global_var:dubois_origin_asia
				global_var:dubois_origin_europe > global_var:dubois_origin_africa
			}
			set_global_variable = dubois_origin_europe_vote
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				global_var:dubois_origin_asia > global_var:dubois_origin_europe
				global_var:dubois_origin_asia > global_var:dubois_origin_africa
			}
			set_global_variable = dubois_origin_asia_vote
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				global_var:dubois_origin_africa > global_var:dubois_origin_asia
				global_var:dubois_origin_africa > global_var:dubois_origin_europe
			}
			set_global_variable = dubois_origin_africa_vote
		}
		else = {
			set_global_variable = dubois_origin_asia_vote
		}
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_global_variable = dubois_origin_europe_vote
		}
		name = dubois.919.g #As expected, Humanity evolved in Europe.
		dubois_small_add_technology = yes
		anthropologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "15"
		}
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_global_variable = dubois_origin_asia_vote
		}
		name = dubois.919.h #All evidences suggest that humanity evolved in Asia.
		lepsius_small_add_technology = yes
		dubois_medium_add_technology = yes
		anthropologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "25"
		}
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_global_variable = dubois_origin_africa_vote
		}
		name = dubois.919.i #'Out of Africa' is an approved thesis now.
		default_option = yes
		lepsius_large_add_technology = yes
		dubois_large_add_technology = yes
		anthropologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "35"
		}
	}

	after = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					this = ROOT 
				}
				has_modifier = dubois_congress_attend_modifier
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.920
				popup = yes
			}
		}
		remove_global_variable = dubois_origin_europe
		remove_global_variable = dubois_origin_asia
		remove_global_variable = dubois_origin_africa
	}
}

#######Extinction of the Dinosaurs######

#Dubois 921: Extinction - Invitation

dubois.921 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.921.t
	desc = dubois.921.d
	flavor = dubois.921.f

	duration = 1

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_extinction_congress.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fossil.dds"

	immediate = {
		var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
			set_variable = dubois_attended_extinction_congress_var
			save_scope_as = dubois_paleontologist_scope
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = dubois.921.g # Invite the leading paleontologist nations
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					this = ROOT 
				}
				has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_var
				OR = {
					var:dubois_fossil >= 10
					dubois_has_dinosaur_skeleton = yes
				}
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.922
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_variable = verrier_astronomer_var
					var:verrier_astronomer_var = {
						has_trait = verrier_astronomer_famous
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_var
					var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
						has_trait = dubois_paleontologist_famous
					}
				}
				has_technology_researched = verrier_astro_physics_tech
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.923
				days = { 3 6 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.924
				days = { 7 14 }
			}
		}
		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.929
			days = 180
		}
	}
}

#Dubois 924: Extinction - Why did the dinosaurs die out?

dubois.924 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.924.t
	desc = dubois.924.d
	flavor = dubois.924.f

	duration = 2

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_extinction_congress.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fossil.dds"

	immediate = {
		var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = dubois_paleontologist_scope
		}
	}

	#Potemkin Congress

	option = { 
		name = dubois.924.a #An asteroid impact was responsible.
		trigger = {
			has_variable = dubois_extinction_asteroid_theory_var
		}
		highlighted_option = yes
		default_option = yes
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = dubois.924.g #The sea level dropped and destroyed habitats
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_variable = dubois_extinction_asteroid_theory_var
			}
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = dubois.924.h #Oxygen contents of Earth's atmosphere rose to levels better suited for birds and mammals
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_variable = dubois_extinction_asteroid_theory_var
			}
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = dubois.924.i #Maladaptive traits
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_variable = dubois_extinction_asteroid_theory_var
			}
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = dubois.924.j #Diminuition of sexual activity
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_variable = dubois_extinction_asteroid_theory_var
			}
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = dubois.924.k #Pathological Gigantism
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_variable = dubois_extinction_asteroid_theory_var
			}

#Dubois 929: Extinction - Decision Host

dubois.929 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.929.t

	desc = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = dubois_extinction_asteroid
			}
			desc = dubois.929.d_asteroid
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = dubois_extinction_climate
			}
			desc = dubois.929.d_climate
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = dubois_extinction_sex
			}
			desc = dubois.929.d_sex
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = dubois_extinction_mammals
			}
			desc = dubois.929.d_mammals
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = dubois_extinction_fat
			}
			desc = dubois.929.d_fat
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = dubois_extinction_stupid
			}
			desc = dubois.929.d_stupid
		}
	}

	flavor = dubois.929.f

	duration = 2

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_extinction_congress.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fossil.dds"

	immediate = {
		var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = dubois_paleontologist_scope
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					has_variable = dubois_extinction_asteroid_theory_var
				}
			}
			set_global_variable = dubois_extinction_asteroid
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					set_global_variable = dubois_extinction_climate
				}
				1 = {
					set_global_variable = dubois_extinction_sex
				}
				1 = {
					set_global_variable = dubois_extinction_mammals
				}
				1 = {
					set_global_variable = dubois_extinction_fat
				}
				1 = {
					set_global_variable = dubois_extinction_stupid
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = dubois.929.g #An asteroid impact was responsible.
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			has_global_variable = dubois_extinction_asteroid
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dubois_extinction_asteroid_theory_var
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = verrier_breakthrough_modifier
				years = 10
			}
		}
		dubois_large_add_technology = yes
		dubois_add_x_academy_progress = {
			AMOUNT = "10"
		}
		paleontologist_experience_gain_effect = {
			AMOUNT = "20"
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = dubois.929.g #Aan awkward theory, but the only one accepted.
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_variable = dubois_extinction_asteroid
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					this = ROOT 
				}
				has_modifier = dubois_congress_attend_modifier
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.930
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

#Dubois 1013: Lion Enclosure
dubois.1013 = {
	type = country_event

    title = dubois.1013.t
    desc = dubois.1013.d
    flavor = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				var:dubois_zoo_lion_flavor_randomizer_var = 1
			}
			desc = dubois.1013.f1
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				var:dubois_zoo_lion_flavor_randomizer_var = 2
			}
			desc = dubois.1013.f2
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				var:dubois_zoo_lion_flavor_randomizer_var = 3
			}
			desc = dubois.1013.f3
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				var:dubois_zoo_lion_flavor_randomizer_var = 4
			}
			desc = dubois.1013.f4
		}
	}

	placement = root

    event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_zoo_afr_lions.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/middleeast/jungle_expedition"
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

    duration = 3

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_role = general
				is_busy = no
				age >= 70
			}
			save_scope_as = dubois_prinz_eugen
		}
		random_list = { #randomizes flavor text
			10 = { 
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_lion_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 1
				}
			}
			10 = { 
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_lion_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 2
				}
			}
			10 = { 
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_lion_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 3
				}
			}
			0 = { 
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							any_scope_character = {
								has_role = general
								is_busy = no
								age >= 70
							}
							NOT = {
								has_variable = dubois_prinz_eugen_var
							}
						}
						add = 70
					}
				}
				set_variable = dubois_prinz_eugen_var
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_lion_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 4
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1012.k #Return to the African Enclosures
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:dubois_zoo_lion_flavor_randomizer_var = 4
			}
			scope:dubois_prinz_eugen = {
				kill_character = yes
			}
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					is_capital = yes
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = dubois_eugen_and_the_lion_modifier
					years = 3
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = zoo_african_enclosures_tt
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.1011
				popup = yes
			}
			remove_variable = dubois_zoo_lion_flavor_randomizer_var
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1011.l #Return to the Main Entrance
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:dubois_zoo_lion_flavor_randomizer_var = 4
			}
			scope:dubois_prinz_eugen = {
				kill_character = yes
			}
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					is_capital = yes
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = dubois_eugen_and_the_lion_modifier
					years = 3
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = zoo_main_entrance_tt
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.1001
				popup = yes
			}
			remove_variable = dubois_zoo_lion_flavor_randomizer_var
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1001.m #Leave the Zoo
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:dubois_zoo_lion_flavor_randomizer_var = 4
			}
			scope:dubois_prinz_eugen = {
				kill_character = yes
			}
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					is_capital = yes
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = dubois_eugen_and_the_lion_modifier
					years = 3
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = leave_zoo_tt
			remove_variable = dubois_visiting_zoo_var
			remove_variable = dubois_zoo_lion_flavor_randomizer_var
		}
	}
}

#Dubois 1036: Platypus Enclosure
dubois.1036 = {
	type = country_event

    title = dubois.1036.t
    desc = dubois.1036.d
    flavor = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				var:dubois_zoo_platypus_flavor_randomizer_var = 1
			}
			desc = dubois.1036.f1
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				var:dubois_zoo_platypus_flavor_randomizer_var = 2
			}
			desc = dubois.1036.f2
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				var:dubois_zoo_platypus_flavor_randomizer_var = 3
			}
			desc = dubois.1036.f3
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_perry_the_platypus_var
				NOT = {
					has_variable = dubois_perry_left_var
				}
			}
			desc = dubois.1036.f4
		}
	}

	placement = root

    event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_animal_platypus.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/middleeast/jungle_expedition"
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

    duration = 3

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_list = { #randomizes flavor text
			8 = {
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_platypus_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 1
				}
			}
			8 = {
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_platypus_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 2
				}
			}
			8 = {
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_platypus_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 3
				}
			}
			1 = {
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_perry_the_platypus_var
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1032.k #Return to the Australian and Oceanian 
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = dubois_perry_the_platypus_var
				}
				AND = {
					has_variable = dubois_perry_the_platypus_var
					has_variable = dubois_perry_left_var
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = zoo_australian_enclosures_tt
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.1031
				popup = yes
			}
			remove_variable = dubois_zoo_platypus_flavor_randomizer_var
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1011.l #Return to the Main Entrance
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = dubois_perry_the_platypus_var
				}
				AND = {
					has_variable = dubois_perry_the_platypus_var
					has_variable = dubois_perry_left_var
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = zoo_main_entrance_tt
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.1001
				popup = yes
			}
			remove_variable = dubois_zoo_platypus_flavor_randomizer_var
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1001.m #Leave the Zoo
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = dubois_perry_the_platypus_var
				}
				AND = {
					has_variable = dubois_perry_the_platypus_var
					has_variable = dubois_perry_left_var
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = leave_zoo_tt
			remove_variable = dubois_visiting_zoo_var
			remove_variable = dubois_zoo_platypus_flavor_randomizer_var
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1032.g #A Platypus? Perry the Platypus!
		trigger = {
			has_variable = dubois_perry_the_platypus_var
			NOT = {
				has_variable = dubois_perry_left_var
			}
		}
		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.1036
			popup = yes
		}
		set_variable = dubois_perry_left_var
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_dubois_zoo
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_unknown_hero_modifier
				years = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

#Dubois 1043: Eurasian Wolf Enclosure
dubois.1043 = {
	type = country_event

    title = dubois.1043.t
    desc = dubois.1043.d
    flavor = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				var:dubois_zoo_wolf_flavor_randomizer_var = 1
			}
			desc = dubois.1043.f1
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				var:dubois_zoo_wolf_flavor_randomizer_var = 2
			}
			desc = dubois.1043.f2
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				var:dubois_zoo_wolf_flavor_randomizer_var = 3
			}
			desc = dubois.1043.f3
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				var:dubois_zoo_wolf_flavor_randomizer_var = 4
			}
			desc = dubois.1043.f4
		}
	}

	placement = root

    event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_animal_wolf.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/middleeast/jungle_expedition"
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

    duration = 3

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_list = { #randomizes flavor text
			10 = {
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_wolf_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 1
				}
			}
			10 = {
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_wolf_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 2
				}
			}
			10 = {
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_wolf_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 3
				}
			}
			0 = { 
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								has_modifier = elgar_prokofiev_great_composer_modifier
								any_scope_state = {
									has_modifier = elgar_prokofiev_performance_modifier
								}
							}
							NOT = {
								has_variable = dubois_prokofiev_and_the_wolf_var
							}
						}
						add = 70
					}
				}
				set_variable = dubois_prokofiev_and_the_wolf_var
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_wolf_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 4
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1042.k #Return to the European Enclosures
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = zoo_european_enclosures_tt
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.1041
				popup = yes
			}
			remove_variable = dubois_zoo_wolf_flavor_randomizer_var
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:dubois_zoo_wolf_flavor_randomizer_var = 4
			}
			elgar_add_x_music_tradition_effect = { AMOUNT = 15 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1011.l #Return to the Main Entrance
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = zoo_main_entrance_tt
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.1001
				popup = yes
			}
			remove_variable = dubois_zoo_wolf_flavor_randomizer_var
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:dubois_zoo_wolf_flavor_randomizer_var = 4
			}
			elgar_add_x_music_tradition_effect = { AMOUNT = 15 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1001.m #Leave the Zoo
		default_option = yes
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = leave_zoo_tt
			remove_variable = dubois_visiting_zoo_var
			remove_variable = dubois_zoo_wolf_flavor_randomizer_var
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:dubois_zoo_wolf_flavor_randomizer_var = 4
			}
			elgar_add_x_music_tradition_effect = { AMOUNT = 15 }
		}
	}
}

#Dubois 1053: Grizzly Bear Enclosure
dubois.1053 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.1053.t
	desc = dubois.1053.d
	flavor = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				var:dubois_zoo_grizzly_flavor_randomizer_var = 1
			}
			desc = dubois.1053.f1
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				var:dubois_zoo_grizzly_flavor_randomizer_var = 2
			}
			desc = dubois.1053.f2
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				var:dubois_zoo_grizzly_flavor_randomizer_var = 3
			}
			desc = dubois.1053.f3
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				var:dubois_zoo_grizzly_flavor_randomizer_var = 4
			}
			desc = dubois.1053.f4
		}
	}

	placement = root

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_animal_grizzly.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/middleeast/jungle_expedition"
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_list = { #randomizes flavor text
			10 = { 
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_grizzly_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 1
				}
			}
			10 = { 
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_grizzly_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 2
				}
			}
			10 = { 
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_grizzly_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 3
				}
			}
			0 = { 
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							any_scope_pop = {
								has_pop_culture = greek
							}
							NOT = {
								country_has_primary_culture = cu:greek
							}
							NOT = {
								has_variable = dubois_new_hercules_var
							}
						}
						add = 70
					}
				}
				set_variable = dubois_new_hercules_var
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_grizzly_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 4
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1052.k #Return to the North American Enclosures
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = zoo_north_american_enclosures_tt
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.1051
				popup = yes
			}
			remove_variable = dubois_zoo_grizzly_flavor_randomizer_var
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:dubois_zoo_grizzly_flavor_randomizer_var = 4
			}
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					is_capital = yes
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = dubois_new_hercules_modifier
					years = 3
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1011.l #Return to the Main Entrance
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = zoo_main_entrance_tt
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.1001
				popup = yes
			}
			remove_variable = dubois_zoo_grizzly_flavor_randomizer_var
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:dubois_zoo_grizzly_flavor_randomizer_var = 4
			}
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					is_capital = yes
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = dubois_new_hercules_modifier
					years = 3
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1001.m #Leave the Zoo
		default_option = yes
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = leave_zoo_tt
			remove_variable = dubois_visiting_zoo_var
			remove_variable = dubois_zoo_grizzly_flavor_randomizer_var
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:dubois_zoo_grizzly_flavor_randomizer_var = 4
			}
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					is_capital = yes
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = dubois_new_hercules_modifier
					years = 3
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Dubois 1055: Florida Panther Enclosure
dubois.1055 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.1055.t
	desc = dubois.1055.d
	flavor = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				var:dubois_zoo_panther_flavor_randomizer_var = 1
			}
			desc = dubois.1055.f1
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				var:dubois_zoo_panther_flavor_randomizer_var = 2
			}
			desc = dubois.1055.f2
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				var:dubois_zoo_panther_flavor_randomizer_var = 3
			}
			desc = dubois.1055.f3
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				var:dubois_zoo_panther_flavor_randomizer_var = 4
			}
			desc = dubois.1055.f4
		}
	}

	placement = root

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_animal_panther.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/middleeast/jungle_expedition"
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = literary
			}
			save_scope_as = manzoni_literary_scope
		}
		random_list = { #randomizes flavor text
			10 = { 
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_panther_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 1
				}
			}
			10 = { 
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_panther_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 2
				}
			}
			10 = { 
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_panther_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 3
				}
			}
			0 = { 
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							any_scope_character = {
								has_trait = literary
							}
							NOT = {
								has_variable = dubois_the_panther_var
							}
						}
						add = 70
					}
				}
				set_variable = dubois_the_panther_var
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_panther_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 4
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1052.k #Return to the North American Enclosures
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = zoo_north_american_enclosures_tt
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.1051
				popup = yes
			}
			remove_variable = dubois_zoo_panther_flavor_randomizer_var
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:dubois_zoo_panther_flavor_randomizer_var = 4
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_the_panther_modifier
				years = 3
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1011.l #Return to the Main Entrance
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = zoo_main_entrance_tt
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.1001
				popup = yes
			}
			remove_variable = dubois_zoo_panther_flavor_randomizer_var
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:dubois_zoo_panther_flavor_randomizer_var = 4
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_the_panther_modifier
				years = 3
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1001.m #Leave the Zoo
		default_option = yes
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = leave_zoo_tt
			remove_variable = dubois_visiting_zoo_var
			remove_variable = dubois_zoo_panther_flavor_randomizer_var
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:dubois_zoo_panther_flavor_randomizer_var = 4
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_the_panther_modifier
				years = 3
			}
		}
	}
}

#Animal Babies

#Dubois.1101: A Baby animal was born
dubois.1101 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.1101.t
	desc = dubois.1101.d
	flavor = dubois.1101.f

	placement = root

	event_image = { #Lion Baby
		trigger = {
			var:dubois_zoo_baby_type = 1
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/zoo_babies/dubois_baby_lion.dds"
	}

	event_image = { #Otter Baby
		trigger = {
			var:dubois_zoo_baby_type = 2
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/zoo_babies/dubois_baby_otter.dds"
	}

	event_image = { #Jaguar Baby
		trigger = {
			var:dubois_zoo_baby_type = 3
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/zoo_babies/dubois_baby_jaguar.dds"
	}

	event_image = { #Koala Baby
		trigger = {
			var:dubois_zoo_baby_type = 4
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/zoo_babies/dubois_baby_koala.dds"
	}

	event_image = { #Panda Baby
		trigger = {
			var:dubois_zoo_baby_type = 5
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/zoo_babies/dubois_baby_panda.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/middleeast/jungle_expedition"
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	duration = 3

	cooldown = {
		years = 25
	}

	trigger = {
		is_player = yes
		NOR = {
			has_modifier = dubois_animal_baby_modifier
			has_global_variable = dubois_no_more_baby_animals_global_var
		}
		any_scope_building = {
			is_building_type = building_dubois_zoo
			level > 0
		}
		OR = {
			has_variable = dubois_zoo_animal_lion
			has_variable = dubois_zoo_animal_otter
			has_variable = dubois_zoo_animal_jaguar
			has_variable = dubois_zoo_animal_koala
			has_variable = dubois_zoo_animal_panda
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_dubois_zoo
			}
			save_scope_as = zoo_state_scope
		}

		random_list = { #randomizes flavor text
			1 = {
				trigger = {
					has_variable = dubois_zoo_animal_lion
				}
				set_variable = { #Lion
					name = dubois_zoo_baby_type
					value = 1
				}
			}
			1 = {
				trigger = {
					has_variable = dubois_zoo_animal_otter
				}
				set_variable = { #Otter
					name = dubois_zoo_baby_type
					value = 2
				}
			}
			1 = {
				trigger = {
					has_variable = dubois_zoo_animal_jaguar
				}
				set_variable = { #Jaguar
					name = dubois_zoo_baby_type
					value = 3
				}
			}
			1 = {
				trigger = {
					has_variable = dubois_zoo_animal_koala
				}
				set_variable = { #Koala
					name = dubois_zoo_baby_type
					value = 4
				}
			}
			1 = {
				trigger = {
					has_variable = dubois_zoo_animal_panda
				}
				set_variable = { #Panda
					name = dubois_zoo_baby_type
					value = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}

	###### Baby names ######
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 1 --> Bubbles
	### Lions ###
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 2 --> Simba (Lion)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 3 --> Zuri (Lion)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 4 --> Kya (Lion)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 5 --> Lwazi (Lion)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 6 --> Nala (Lion)
	### Otters ###
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 7 --> Otto (Otter)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 8 --> Oskar (Otter)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 9 --> Alice (Otter)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 10 --> Max (Otter)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 11 --> Freja (Otter)
	### Jaguar ###
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 12 --> Cihuacoatl  (Jaguar)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 13 --> Yaotl  (Jaguar)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 14 --> Feliz (Jaguar)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 15 --> Santiago (Jaguar)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 16 --> Isabella (Jaguar)
	### Koala ###
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 17 --> Alfie (Koala)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 18 --> Pippa (Koala)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 19 --> Uki (Koala)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 20 --> Milo (Koala)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 21 --> Victoria (Koala)
	### Panda ###
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 22 --> Meng Xiang (Panda)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 23 --> Xiao Qi Ji (Panda)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 24 --> Fu Ni (Panda)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 25 --> Po (Panda)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 26 --> Tao Tao (Panda)

	option = {
		name = dubois.1101.bubbles #Bubbles

		set_variable = {
			name = dubois_baby_animal_name
			value = 1
		}
		
		scope:zoo_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_animal_baby_modifier
				months = 12
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1011.lion_name_1 #Simba (Lion)

		trigger = {
			var:dubois_zoo_baby_type = 1
		}

		set_variable = {
			name = dubois_baby_animal_name
			value = 2
		}

		scope:zoo_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_animal_baby_modifier
				months = 12
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1011.lion_name_2 #Zuri (Lion)

		trigger = {
			var:dubois_zoo_baby_type = 1
		}

		set_variable = {
			name = dubois_baby_animal_name
			value = 3
		}

		scope:zoo_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_animal_baby_modifier
				months = 12
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1011.lion_name_3 #Kya (Lion)

		trigger = {
			var:dubois_zoo_baby_type = 1
		}

		set_variable = {
			name = dubois_baby_animal_name
			value = 4
		}
		
		scope:zoo_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_animal_baby_modifier
				months = 12
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1011.lion_name_4 #Lwazi (Lion)

		trigger = {
			var:dubois_zoo_baby_type = 1
		}

		set_variable = {
			name = dubois_baby_animal_name
			value = 5
		}

		scope:zoo_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_animal_baby_modifier
				months = 12
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1011.lion_name_5 #Nala (Lion)

		trigger = {
			var:dubois_zoo_baby_type = 1
		}

		set_variable = {
			name = dubois_baby_animal_name
			value = 6
		}

		scope:zoo_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_animal_baby_modifier
				months = 12
			}
		}

#Dubois 1210: [Scope Animal] in [Scope State] is endangered

dubois.1210 = {
	type = state_event

	title = dubois.1210.t
	desc = dubois.1210.d
	flavor = dubois.1210.f

	placement = root

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_habitat_destruction.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1210.g #We have to protect those animals!
		default_option = yes
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = dubois_endangered_habitat_tt
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_habitat_endangered_modifier
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_habitat_endangered_timer_modifier
				years = 10
			}
		}
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_modifier = dubois_habitat_protection_path_modifier
					}
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = dubois_habitat_protection_path_modifier
					years = 5
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_technology_researched = dubois_genetics_tech
					is_ai = yes
				}
				is_homeland_of_country_cultures = owner
				is_incorporated = yes
			}
			start_building_construction = building_dubois_national_park
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
			modifier = {
				trigger = { 
					owner = {
						ig:ig_intelligentsia = {
							is_in_government = yes
						}
					}
				}
				add = 1000
			}
			modifier = {
				trigger = {
					owner = {
						ig:ig_rural_folk = {
							is_in_government = yes
						}
					}
				}
				add = 1000
			}
			modifier = {
				trigger = {
					owner = {
						ig:ig_landowners = {
							is_in_government = yes
						}
					}
				}
				add = 1000
			}
			modifier = {
				trigger = {
					owner = {
						ruler = {
							OR = {
								is_interest_group_type = ig_intelligentsia
								is_interest_group_type = ig_rural_folk
								is_interest_group_type = ig_landowners
							}
						}
					}
				}
				add = 1000
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1210.h #Progres above everything else!
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = dubois_endangered_habitat_tt
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_habitat_endangered_modifier
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_habitat_endangered_timer_modifier
				years = 10
			}
		}
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_modifier = dubois_habitat_destruction_path_modifier
					}
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = dubois_habitat_destruction_path_modifier
					years = 5
				}
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				trigger = {
					owner = {
						ig:ig_industrialists = {
							is_in_government = yes
						}
					}
				}
				add = 1000
			}
			modifier = {
				trigger = {
					owner = {
						ig:ig_trade_unions = {
							is_in_government = yes
						}
					}
				}
				add = 1000
			}
			modifier = {
				trigger = {
					owner = {
						ruler = {
							OR = {
								is_interest_group_type = ig_industrialists
								is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions
							}
						}
					}
				}
				add = 1000
			}
		}
	}
}

#Dubois 1250: Yosemite National Park

dubois.1250 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.1250.t
	desc = dubois.1250.d
	flavor = dubois.1250.f

	placement = scope:yosemite_state_scope

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_nature_reserve_yosemite.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = dubois_yosemite_event_var
		}
		year >= 1890
		OR = {
			c:USA ?= this
			c:CAL ?= this
			was_formed_from = USA
			was_formed_from = CAL
		}
		p:x0AF8FD = {
			owner = root
		}
		any_scope_state = {
			state_region = s:STATE_CALIFORNIA
			NOT = {
				has_building = building_dubois_national_park
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_CALIFORNIA
			}
			save_scope_as = yosemite_state_scope
		}
		set_variable = dubois_yosemite_event_var
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1250.g #This is a great idea!
		default_option = yes
		
		scope:yosemite_state_scope = {
			start_building_construction = building_dubois_national_park
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1250.h #Actually, this looks like a great place for mining!

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

#Dubois 1251: The last Wisents

dubois.1251 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.1251.t
	desc = dubois.1251.d
	flavor = dubois.1251.f

	placement = scope:bialowieza_state_scope

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_nature_reserve_bialowieza.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = dubois_bialowieza_event_var
		}
		year >= 1860
		has_state_in_state_region = STATE_BREST
		any_scope_state = {
			state_region = s:STATE_BREST
			has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_wisent_habitat
			NOT = {
				has_building = building_dubois_national_park
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_BREST
			}
			save_scope_as = bialowieza_state_scope
		}
		set_variable = dubois_bialowieza_event_var
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1251.g #We need to protect the Wisent!
		default_option = yes
		
		scope:bialowieza_state_scope = {
			start_building_construction = building_dubois_national_park
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1251.h #This forest is perfect for logging.

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				trigger = {
					ruler = {
						interest_group = { 
							OR = {
								is_interest_group_type = ig_landowners
								is_interest_group_type = ig_industrialists
							}
						}
					}
				}
				add = 25
			}
		}
	}
}

#Dubois 1252: A Royal Hunting Reserve in Gran Paradiso?

dubois.1252 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.1252.t
	desc = dubois.1252.d
	flavor = dubois.1252.f

	placement = scope:gran_paradiso_state_scope

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_natue_reserve_gran_paradiso.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = dubois_gran_paradiso_global_var
		}
		has_law = law_type:law_monarchy
		OR = {
			year >= 1856
			ruler = {
				interest_group = { 
					OR = {
						is_interest_group_type = ig_intelligentsia
						is_interest_group_type = ig_rural_folk
					}
				}
			}
		}
		any_scope_state = {
			state_region = s:STATE_PIEDMONT
			has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_ibex_habitat
			NOT = {
				has_building = building_dubois_national_park
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_PIEDMONT
			}
			save_scope_as = gran_paradiso_state_scope
		}
		set_global_variable = dubois_gran_paradiso_global_var
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1252.g #Found the Reserve immediately!
		default_option = yes
		
		scope:gran_paradiso_state_scope = {
			start_building_construction = building_dubois_national_park
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1252.h #Maybe later...

		custom_tooltip = {
			text = dubois_gran_paradiso_tt
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

#Dubois 1301: Choose a Nature Reserve to breed Exotic Animals

dubois.1301 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.1301.t
	desc = dubois.1301.d

	placement = root

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_natue_reserve_gran_paradiso.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		#Triggered by desicion
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_state = {
					any_scope_building = {
						is_building_type = building_dubois_national_park
						level > 0
					}
					OR = {
						dubois_polar_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_europe_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_north_america_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_south_america_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_africa_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_asia_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_australia_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
					}
				}
			}
			random_scope_state = { #This sets the first state as a scope
				limit = {
					any_scope_building = {
						is_building_type = building_dubois_national_park
						level > 0
					}
					OR = {
						dubois_polar_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_europe_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_north_america_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_south_america_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_africa_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_asia_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_australia_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				save_scope_as = breeding_state_1_scope
			}
			set_variable = { #Used to display the amount of Options
				name = dubois_number_of_states_var
				value = 1
			}
		}
		if = { #Checks if a second state is possible
			limit = {
				any_scope_state = {
					NOT = { this = scope:breeding_state_1_scope }
					any_scope_building = {
						is_building_type = building_dubois_national_park
						level > 0
					}
					OR = {
						dubois_polar_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_europe_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_north_america_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_south_america_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_africa_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_asia_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_australia_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
					}
				}
			}
			random_scope_state = { #Sets the second state if possible
				limit = {
					NOT = { this = scope:breeding_state_1_scope }
					any_scope_building = {
						is_building_type = building_dubois_national_park
						level > 0
					}
					OR = {
						dubois_polar_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_europe_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_north_america_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_south_america_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_africa_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_asia_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_australia_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				save_scope_as = breeding_state_2_scope
			}
			change_variable = { #Used to display the amount of Options
				name = dubois_number_of_states_var
				add = 1
			}
		}
		if = { #Checks if a third state is possible
			limit = {
				any_scope_state = {
					NOR = {
						this = scope:breeding_state_1_scope
						this = scope:breeding_state_2_scope
					}
					any_scope_building = {
						is_building_type = building_dubois_national_park
						level > 0
					}
					OR = {
						dubois_polar_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_europe_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_north_america_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_south_america_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_africa_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_asia_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_australia_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
					}
				}
			}
			random_scope_state = { #Sets the third state if possible
				limit = {
					NOR = {
						this = scope:breeding_state_1_scope
						this = scope:breeding_state_2_scope
					}
					any_scope_building = {
						is_building_type = building_dubois_national_park
						level > 0
					}
					OR = {
						dubois_polar_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_europe_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_north_america_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_south_america_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_africa_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_asia_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
						dubois_australia_breeding_possible_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				save_scope_as = breeding_state_3_scope
			}
			change_variable = { #Used to display the amount of Options
				name = dubois_number_of_states_var
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1301.g #[breeding_state_1_scope]
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			var:dubois_number_of_states_var > 0
		}
		
		set_variable = { #Sets the state as a variable to access it later.
			name = dubois_breeding_state_var
			value = scope:breeding_state_1_scope
		}

		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.1302
			popup = yes
		}

		remove_variable = dubois_number_of_states_var
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1301.h #[breeding_state_2_scope]
		trigger = {
			var:dubois_number_of_states_var > 1
		}

		set_variable = { #Sets the state as a variable to access it later.
			name = dubois_breeding_state_var
			value = scope:breeding_state_2_scope
		}

		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.1302
			popup = yes
		}

		remove_variable = dubois_number_of_states_var
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1301.i #[breeding_state_3_scope]
		trigger = { #Sets the state as a variable to access it later.
			var:dubois_number_of_states_var > 2
		}

		set_variable = {
			name = dubois_breeding_state_var
			value = scope:breeding_state_3_scope
		}

		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.1302
			popup = yes
		}

		remove_variable = dubois_number_of_states_var
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1301.j #Nevermind
		
		remove_variable = dubois_number_of_states_var
		remove_variable = dubois_breeding_animals_var

		custom_tooltip = dubois_nope_out_breeding_tt

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

#Dubois 1302: Choose an Exotic Animal to breed

dubois.1302 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.1302.t
	desc = dubois.1302.d

	placement = var:dubois_breeding_state_var

	event_image = { 
		trigger = {
			var:dubois_breeding_state_var = {
				state_is_in_europe = yes
			}
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_nature_reserve_europe.dds"
	}
	event_image = { 
		trigger = {
			var:dubois_breeding_state_var = {
				OR = {
					state_is_in_north_america = yes
					region = sr:region_mexico
				}
			}
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_nature_reserve_north_america.dds"
	}
	event_image = { 
		trigger = {
			var:dubois_breeding_state_var = {
				OR = {
					state_is_in_south_america = yes
					region = sr:region_central_america
					region = sr:region_caribbean
				}
			}
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_nature_reserve_africa.dds"
	}
	event_image = { 
		trigger = {
			var:dubois_breeding_state_var = {
				OR = {
					state_is_in_africa = yes
				}
			}
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_nature_reserve_asia.dds"
	}
	event_image = { 
		trigger = {
			var:dubois_breeding_state_var = {
				OR = {
					state_is_in_middle_east = yes
					state_is_in_central_asia = yes
					state_is_in_india = yes
					state_is_in_east_asia = yes
					state_is_in_southeast_asia = yes
				}
			}
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_nature_reserve_asia.dds"
	}
	event_image = { 
		trigger = {
			var:dubois_breeding_state_var = {
				region = sr:region_oceania
			}
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_nature_reserve_australia_oceania.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		#Triggered by Dubois 1301: Choose a Nature Reserve to breed Exotic Animals
	}

	immediate = {
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1302.polar #Polar Bears
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			var:dubois_breeding_state_var = {
				NOT = {
					has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_polar_habitat
				}
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_type = building_dubois_national_park
					level > 0
				}
				OR = {
					state_region = s:STATE_ICELAND
					state_region = s:STATE_GREENLAND
					state_region = s:STATE_NORTHERN_NORWAY
					state_region = s:STATE_NENETSIA
					state_region = s:STATE_OB
					state_region = s:STATE_UPPER_YENISEYSK
					state_region = s:STATE_YAKUTSK
					state_region = s:STATE_CHUKOTKA
					state_region = s:STATE_KAMCHATKA
					state_region = s:STATE_ALASKA
					state_region = s:STATE_YUKON_TERRITORY
					state_region = s:STATE_NORTHWEST_TERRITORIES
					state_region = s:STATE_NUNAVUT
					state_region = s:STATE_MANITOBA
					state_region = s:STATE_ONTARIO
					state_region = s:STATE_QUEBEC
					state_region = s:STATE_NEWFOUNDLAND
				}
			}
			has_variable = dubois_zoo_animal_polar
		}
		
		set_variable = dubois_breeding_polar_var

		custom_tooltip = {
			text = dubois.1302.option_tt
			add_journal_entry = {
				type = je_animal_breeding
				target = var:dubois_breeding_state_var
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1302.grizzly #Grizzly Bears
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			var:dubois_breeding_state_var = {
				NOT = {
					has_state_trait = dubois_state_trait_grizzly_habitat
				}
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_type = building_dubois_national_park
					level > 0
				}
				OR = {
					state_is_in_north_america = yes
					region = sr:region_mexico
				}
			}

				}

					state_is_in_central_asia = yes
