					state_is_in_east_asia = yes
					state_is_in_southeast_asia = yes
				}
			}
			has_variable = dubois_zoo_animal_orangutan
		}

#Dubois 1311: Hidden Event to calculate change for the animal population
dubois.1311 = {
	type = country_event

	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = dubois_last_animal_polpulation
			value = var:dubois_breeding_animal_amount_var
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = dubois_breeding_animal_amount_var
			multiply = dubois_breeding_multiplier
		}
		round_variable = {
			name = dubois_breeding_animal_amount_var
			nearest = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dubois_animal_breeding_change_var
			value = var:dubois_breeding_animal_amount_var
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = dubois_animal_breeding_change_var
			subtract = var:dubois_last_animal_polpulation
		}

		post_notification = dubois_animal_breeding_notification
	}
}

#Dubois 1322: Breeding the [Animal] failed

dubois.1322 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.1322.t
	desc = dubois.1322.d
	flavor = dubois.1322.f

	placement = root

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_natue_reserve_gran_paradiso.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		#Triggered by JE failure
	}

	immediate = {
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1322.g #What a sad day.
		default_option = yes
		
		#This Effect removes all Variables that are no longer required
		dubois_remove_breeding_effect = yes
	}
}

#Dubois 2001: Main

dubois.2001 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.2001.t
	desc = dubois.2001.d

	flavor = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_var 
			}
			desc = dubois.2001.f_paleontologist
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_var
				}
			}
			desc = dubois.2001.f_no_paleontologist
		}
	}

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_paleontological_collection.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fossil.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_var 
			}
			var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
				save_scope_as = dubois_paleontologist_scope
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Visit the Paleontologist
		name = dubois.2001.i
		trigger = {
			dubois_has_paleontologist = yes
		}

		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.2011
			popup = yes
		}
	}

	option = {	#Visit Special Fossils
		name = dubois.2001.j
		trigger = {
			dubois_has_special_fossil = yes
		}

		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.2021
			popup = yes
		}
	}

	option = {	#Visit Dinosaur Bones
		name = dubois.2001.l
		trigger = {
			dubois_has_dinosaur_bone = yes
		}

		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.2041
			popup = yes
		}
	}

	option = {	#Visit Dinosaur Skeletons
		name = dubois.2001.m
		trigger = {
			dubois_has_dinosaur_skeleton = yes
		}

		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.2051
			popup = yes
		}
	}

	option = {	#Leave the Fossil Collection
		name = dubois.2001.g
		default_option = yes
		remove_variable = dubois_visiting_fossils_var

		custom_tooltip = dubois_leave_fossils_tt
	}
}

#Dubois 2011: Paleontologist

dubois.2011 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.2011.t
	desc = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_in_north_america_var
			}
			desc = dubois.2011.d_north_america
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_in_south_america_var
			}
			desc = dubois.2011.d_south_america
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_in_europe_var
			}
			desc = dubois.2011.d_europe
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_in_africa_var
			}
			desc = dubois.2011.d_africa
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_in_asia_var
			}
			desc = dubois.2011.d_asia
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_in_europe_var
			}
			desc = dubois.2011.d_australia
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_modifier = dubois_paleontologist_travell_to_location_modifier
			}
			desc = dubois.2011.d_to_location
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_modifier = dubois_paleontologist_travell_from_location_modifier
			}
			desc = dubois.2011.d_from_location
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				NOR = {
					has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_in_north_america_var
					has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_in_south_america_var
					has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_in_europe_var
					has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_in_africa_var
					has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_in_asia_var
					has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_in_australia_var
					has_modifier = dubois_paleontologist_travell_to_location_modifier
					has_modifier = dubois_paleontologist_travell_from_location_modifier
				}
			}
			desc = dubois.2011.d_default
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				NOR = {
					has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_in_north_america_var
					has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_in_south_america_var
					has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_in_europe_var
					has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_in_africa_var
					has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_in_asia_var
					has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_in_australia_var
					has_modifier = dubois_paleontologist_travell_to_location_modifier
					has_modifier = dubois_paleontologist_travell_from_location_modifier
				}
				scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope = {
					is_busy = yes
				}
			}
			desc = dubois.2011.d_other
		}
	}
	flavor = dubois.2011.f

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fossil.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = dubois_paleontologist_scope
		}
	}

	option = {	#Return to the Main Hall
		name = dubois.2001.h
		default_option = yes

		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.2001
			popup = yes
		}
	}
	option = {	#Leave the Fossil Collection
		name = dubois.2001.g
		remove_variable = dubois_visiting_fossils_var

		custom_tooltip = dubois_leave_fossils_tt
	}
}

	flavor = dubois.2102.f

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fossil.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = dubois_paleontologist_scope
		}
	}

	option = {	#And all the trouble for that?
		name = dubois.2102.g
		default_option = yes
		scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_exhausted_paleontologist_modifier
				years = 1
			}
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = no
		}
	}

	after = {
		remove_dubois_remount_dinosaur_effect = yes
	}
}

#Dubois 2103: Worse Remount

dubois.2103 = {
	type = country_event

	desc = dubois.2103.d

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = dubois_paleontologist_scope
		}
	}

	option = {	#That fool made it worse!
		name = dubois.2103.g
		default_option = yes
		dubois_add_worse_dinosaur_skeleton = yes
		scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_exhausted_paleontologist_modifier
				years = 1
			}
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = no
		}
	}

	after = {
		remove_dubois_remount_dinosaur_effect = yes
	}
}

######North American Dinosaur Collection######

#Dubois 2111: North American Dinosaurs

dubois.2111 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.2111.t
	desc = dubois.2111.d

	flavor = dubois.2111.f

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_dinosaur_north_america.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fossil.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	option = {	#Visit Ankylosaurus
		name = dubois.2111.g
		trigger = {
			has_variable = dubois_ankylosaurus_var
		}

		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.2112
			popup = yes
		}
	}
	option = {	#Visit Diplodocus
		name = dubois.2111.h
		trigger = {
			has_variable = dubois_diplodocus_var
		}

		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.2113
			popup = yes
		}
	}
	option = {	#Visit Triceratops
		name = dubois.2111.i
		trigger = {
			has_variable = dubois_triceratops_var
		}

		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.2114
			popup = yes
		}
	}
	option = {	#Visit Tyrannosaurus Rex
		name = dubois.2111.j
		trigger = {
			has_variable = dubois_tyrannosaurus_var
		}

		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.2115
			popup = yes
		}
	}

	option = {	#Visit Stegosaurus
		name = dubois.2111.k
		trigger = {
			has_variable = dubois_stegosaurus_var
		}

		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.2116
			popup = yes
		}
	}

	option = {	#Return to the Main Hall
		name = dubois.2001.h
		default_option = yes

		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.2001
			popup = yes
		}
	}
	option = {	#Leave the Fossil Collection
		name = dubois.2001.g
		remove_variable = dubois_visiting_fossils_var

		custom_tooltip = dubois_leave_fossils_tt
	}
}

#Dubois 2112: Ankylosaurus

dubois.2112 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.2112.t
	desc = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_perfect_ankylosaurus_var
			}
			desc = dubois.2112.d_perfect_dinosaur
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_imperfect_ankylosaurus_var
			}
			desc = dubois.2112.d_imperfect_dinosaur
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_poor_ankylosaurus_var
			}
			desc = dubois.2112.d_poor_dinosaur
		}
	}

	flavor = dubois.2112.f

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_dinosaur_skeleton.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fossil.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_var 
			}
			var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
				save_scope_as = dubois_paleontologist_scope
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Return to North America Section
		name = dubois.2112.h

		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.2111
			popup = yes
		}
	}
	option = {	#Return to the Main Hall
		name = dubois.2001.h
		default_option = yes

		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.2001
			popup = yes
		}
	}
	option = {	#Leave the Fossil Collection
		name = dubois.2001.g
		remove_variable = dubois_visiting_fossils_var

		custom_tooltip = dubois_leave_fossils_tt
	}
}

#Dubois 2171: Construct Dinosaur Skeleton

dubois.2171 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.2171.t
	desc = dubois.2171.d

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_collection_dinosaur_bones.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fossil.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	immediate = {
	}

	option = {	#Construct North American Dinosaur
		name = dubois.2041.h
		trigger = {
			var:dubois_north_american_dinosaur_bone >= 5
			NAND = {
				has_variable = dubois_ankylosaurus_var
				has_variable = dubois_diplodocus_var
				has_variable = dubois_triceratops_var
				has_variable = dubois_tyrannosaurus_var
				has_variable = dubois_stegosaurus_var
			}
			has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_var
			var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
				is_busy = no
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = dubois_exhausted_paleontologist_modifier
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = dubois_construct_north_american_dinosaur_var
		dubois_construct_dinosaur_effect = yes
		dubois_construct_north_american_dinosaur = yes
		var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.2001
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	#Construct South American Dinosaur
		name = dubois.2041.i
		trigger = {
			var:dubois_south_american_dinosaur_bone >= 5
			NAND = {
				has_variable = dubois_antarctosaurus_var
				has_variable = dubois_argyrosaurus_var
			}
			has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_var
			var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
				is_busy = no
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = dubois_exhausted_paleontologist_modifier
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = dubois_construct_south_american_dinosaur_var
		dubois_construct_dinosaur_effect = yes
		dubois_construct_south_american_dinosaur = yes
		var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.2001
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	#Construct European Dinosaur
		name = dubois.2041.j
		trigger = {
			var:dubois_european_dinosaur_bone >= 5
			NAND = {
				has_variable = dubois_iguanodon_var
				has_variable = dubois_plateosaurus_var
			}
			has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_var
			var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
				is_busy = no
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = dubois_exhausted_paleontologist_modifier
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = dubois_construct_european_dinosaur_var
		dubois_construct_dinosaur_effect = yes
		dubois_construct_european_dinosaur = yes
		var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.2001
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	#Construct African Dinosaur
		name = dubois.2041.k
		trigger = {
			var:dubois_african_dinosaur_bone >= 5
			NAND = {
				has_variable = dubois_giraffatitan_var
				#has_variable = dubois_melanorosaurus_var
				has_variable = dubois_spinosaurus_var
			}
			has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_var
			var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
				is_busy = no
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = dubois_exhausted_paleontologist_modifier
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = dubois_construct_african_dinosaur_var
		dubois_construct_dinosaur_effect = yes
		dubois_construct_african_dinosaur = yes
		var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.2001
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	#Construct Asian Dinosaur
		name = dubois.2041.l
		trigger = {
			var:dubois_asian_dinosaur_bone >= 5
			NAND = {
				has_variable = dubois_psittacosaurus_var
				has_variable = dubois_velociraptor_var
			}
			has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_var
			var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
				is_busy = no
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = dubois_exhausted_paleontologist_modifier
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = dubois_construct_asian_dinosaur_var
		dubois_construct_dinosaur_effect = yes
		dubois_construct_asian_dinosaur = yes
		var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.2001
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	#Construct Australian Dinosaur
		name = dubois.2041.m
		trigger = {
			var:dubois_australian_dinosaur_bone >= 5
			NAND = {
				has_variable = dubois_muttaburrasaurus_var
				has_variable = dubois_rhoetosaurus_var
			}

			}
		}
		set_variable = dubois_construct_australian_dinosaur_var
		dubois_construct_dinosaur_effect = yes
		dubois_construct_australian_dinosaur = yes
		var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.2001
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Do not construct any Dinosaur Skeletons.
		name = dubois.2171.g
		default_option = yes
		custom_tooltip = dubois.2171.g_tt
	}

	after = {
		remove_variable = mr_mount_dinosaur_skeleton_button_var
	}
}

#Dubois 2181: Remount Dinosaur Skeleton

dubois.2181 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.2181.a
	desc = dubois.2181.d

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_dinosaur_skeleton.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fossil.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	immediate = {
	}

	option = {	#Remount Ankylosaurus
		name = dubois.2181.h
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_variable = dubois_imperfect_ankylosaurus_var
				has_variable = dubois_poor_ankylosaurus_var
			}
			has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_var
			var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
				is_busy = no
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = dubois_exhausted_paleontologist_modifier
				}
			}
		}
		var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
		set_variable = dubois_remount_ankylosaurus_var
		dubois_remount_dinosaur_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.2001
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}
